country_event = { #The Question of Language
	
	id = dg_miaphysite.011
	title = dg_miaphysite.011.t
	desc = dg_miaphysite.011.d
	picture = catholic_church_council
	
	trigger = {
		has_country_flag = miaphysite_council
		advisor = theologian
		check_variable = { which = miaphysite_council_topics value = 1 }
		NOT = { has_country_flag = miaphysite_agreement_language }
	}
	
	mean_time_to_happen = {
		
		months = 25
		
		modifier = {
			OR = {
				has_country_modifier = unhappy_church_powerful
				has_country_modifier = unhappy_church_strong
				has_country_modifier = unhappy_church_moderate
				has_country_modifier = unhappy_church_weak
				has_country_modifier = unhappy_church_impotent
			}
			factor = 1.4
		}
		modifier = {
			OR = {
				has_country_modifier = religious_scandal_country_strong
				has_country_modifier = religious_scandal_country
				has_country_modifier = religious_scandal_country_weak
			}
			factor = 2
		}
		modifier = {
			theologian = 2
			factor = 0.7
		}
		modifier = {
			theologian = 3
			factor = 0.7
		}
		modifier = {
			has_country_modifier = union_of_churches
			factor = 0.5
		}
	}
	
	immediate = {
		clr_country_flag = miaphysite_council_falters
		hidden_effect = {
			change_variable = { which = miaphysite_council_topics value = -1 }
			set_country_flag = miaphysite_agreement_language
			set_country_flag = miaphysite_agreement_ratification_needed
			if = {
				limit = { theologian = 3 }
				change_variable = { which = union_of_churches_minority_support value = 0.25 }
				change_variable = { which = union_of_churches_state_support value = 0.25 }
			}
			if = {
				limit = { theologian = 2 }
				change_variable = { which = union_of_churches_minority_support value = 0.25 }
				change_variable = { which = union_of_churches_state_support value = 0.25 }
			}
		}
	}
	
	option = {
		name = dg_miaphysite.011.a #$PRIMARY_CULTURE$ liturgy and bible
		ai_chance = { factor = 40 }
		add_patriarch_authority = 0.05
		add_piety = -0.05
		set_country_flag = single_liturgy_allowed
		#People's reaction
		dg_add_prestige_small = yes
		if = {
			limit = { piety = 0.60 }
			add_adm_power = 20
			if = {
				limit = { NOT = { stability = 0 } }
				random = { chance = 25 add_stability_1 = yes }
			}
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = { piety = 0.20 }
			add_adm_power = 16
			if = {
				limit = { NOT = { stability = 0 } }
				random = { chance = 20 add_stability_1 = yes }
			}
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = { piety = -0.20 }
			add_adm_power = 12
			if = {
				limit = { NOT = { stability = 0 } }
				random = { chance = 15 add_stability_1 = yes }
			}
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = { piety = -0.60 }
			add_adm_power = 8
			if = {
				limit = { NOT = { stability = 0 } }
				random = { chance = 10 add_stability_1 = yes }
			}
		}
		else = {
			add_adm_power = 4
			if = {
				limit = { NOT = { stability = 0 } }
				random = { chance = 5 add_stability_1 = yes }
			}
		}
		#Church's reaction
		if = {
			limit = { patriarch_authority = 0.80 }
			add_legitimacy = 10
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = { patriarch_authority = 0.60 }
			add_legitimacy = 8
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = { patriarch_authority = 0.40 }
			add_legitimacy = 6
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = { patriarch_authority = 0.20 }
			add_legitimacy = 4
		}
		else = {
			add_legitimacy = 2
		}
		trigger_switch = {
			on_trigger = has_country_modifier
			unhappy_church_powerful = {
				remove_country_modifier = unhappy_church_powerful
			}
			unhappy_church_strong = {
				remove_country_modifier = unhappy_church_strong
			}
			unhappy_church_moderate = {
				remove_country_modifier = unhappy_church_moderate
			}
			unhappy_church_weak = {
				remove_country_modifier = unhappy_church_weak
			}
			unhappy_church_impotent = {
				remove_country_modifier = unhappy_church_impotent
			}
		}
		hidden_effect = { change_variable = { which = union_of_churches_state_support value = 1 } }
		if = {
			limit = { NOT = { check_variable = { which = miaphysite_council_topics value = 1 } } }
			country_event = { id = dg_miaphysite.015 days = 10 }
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = dg_miaphysite.011.b #Hierarchy in $PRIMARY_CULTURE$, services in local language
		ai_chance = { factor = 30 }
		#People's reaction
		dg_reduce_legitimacy_large = yes
		if = {
			limit = { piety = 0.60 }
			random = { chance = 50 subtract_stability_1 = yes }
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = { piety = 0.20 }
			random = { chance = 40 subtract_stability_1 = yes }
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = { piety = -0.20 }
			random = { chance = 30 subtract_stability_1 = yes }
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = { piety = -0.60 }
			random = { chance = 20 subtract_stability_1 = yes }
		}
		else = {
			random = { chance = 10 subtract_stability_1 = yes }
		}
		#Church's reaction
		if = {
			limit = { patriarch_authority = 0.80 }
			add_country_modifier = { name = unhappy_church_powerful duration = 1000 }
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = { patriarch_authority = 0.60 }
			add_country_modifier = { name = unhappy_church_strong duration = 1000 }
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = { patriarch_authority = 0.40 }
			add_country_modifier = { name = unhappy_church_moderate duration = 1000 }
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = { patriarch_authority = 0.20 }
			add_country_modifier = { name = unhappy_church_weak duration = 1000 }
		}
		else = {
			add_country_modifier = { name = unhappy_church_impotent duration = 1000 }
		}
		if = {
			limit = { NOT = { check_variable = { which = miaphysite_council_topics value = 1 } } }
			country_event = { id = dg_miaphysite.015 days = 10 }
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = dg_miaphysite.011.c #Allow the local tongue to be used
		ai_chance = { factor = 30 }
		add_patriarch_authority = -0.05
		add_piety = 0.05
		set_country_flag = local_liturgy_allowed
		#People's reaction
		if = {
			limit = { piety = 0.60 }
			subtract_stability_1 = yes
			add_legitimacy = -20
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = { piety = 0.20 }
			random = { chance = 80 subtract_stability_1 = yes }
			add_legitimacy = -16
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = { piety = -0.20 }
			random = { chance = 60 subtract_stability_1 = yes }
			add_legitimacy = -12
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = { piety = -0.60 }
			random = { chance = 40 subtract_stability_1 = yes }
			add_legitimacy = -8
		}
		else = {
			random = { chance = 20 subtract_stability_1 = yes }
			add_legitimacy = -4
		}
		#Church's reaction
		if = {
			limit = { patriarch_authority = 0.80 }
			add_country_modifier = { name = religious_scandal_country_strong duration = 2000 }
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = { patriarch_authority = 0.60 }
			add_country_modifier = { name = religious_scandal_country_strong duration = 1000 }
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = { patriarch_authority = 0.40 }
			add_country_modifier = { name = religious_scandal_country duration = 2000 }
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = { patriarch_authority = 0.20 }
			add_country_modifier = { name = religious_scandal_country_weak duration = 2000 }
		}
		else = {
			add_country_modifier = { name = religious_scandal_country_weak duration = 1000 }
		}
		hidden_effect = { change_variable = { which = union_of_churches_minority_support value = 1 } }
		if = {
			limit = { NOT = { check_variable = { which = miaphysite_council_topics value = 1 } } }
			country_event = { id = dg_miaphysite.015 days = 10 }
		}
	}
}

country_event = { #The Question of Patriarchs
	
	id = dg_miaphysite.012
	title = dg_miaphysite.012.t
	desc = dg_miaphysite.012.d
	picture = catholic_church_council
	
	trigger = {
		has_country_flag = miaphysite_council
		advisor = theologian
		check_variable = { which = miaphysite_council_topics value = 1 }
		NOT = { has_country_flag = miaphysite_agreement_patriarchs }
	}
	
	mean_time_to_happen = {
		
		months = 25
		
		modifier = {
			OR = {
				has_country_modifier = unhappy_church_powerful
				has_country_modifier = unhappy_church_strong
				has_country_modifier = unhappy_church_moderate
				has_country_modifier = unhappy_church_weak
				has_country_modifier = unhappy_church_impotent
			}
			factor = 1.4
		}
		modifier = {
			OR = {
				has_country_modifier = religious_scandal_country_strong
				has_country_modifier = religious_scandal_country
				has_country_modifier = religious_scandal_country_weak
			}
			factor = 2
		}
		modifier = {
			theologian = 2
			factor = 0.7
		}
		modifier = {
			theologian = 3
			factor = 0.7
		}
		modifier = {
			has_country_modifier = union_of_churches
			factor = 0.5
		}
	}
	
	immediate = {
		clr_country_flag = miaphysite_council_falters
		hidden_effect = {
			change_variable = { which = miaphysite_council_topics value = -1 }
			set_country_flag = miaphysite_agreement_patriarchs
			set_country_flag = miaphysite_agreement_ratification_needed
			if = {
				limit = { theologian = 3 }
				change_variable = { which = union_of_churches_minority_support value = 0.25 }
				change_variable = { which = union_of_churches_state_support value = 0.25 }
			}
			if = {
				limit = { theologian = 2 }
				change_variable = { which = union_of_churches_minority_support value = 0.25 }
				change_variable = { which = union_of_churches_state_support value = 0.25 }
			}
		}
	}
	
	option = {
		name = dg_miaphysite.012.a #Recognize the $COUNTRY_RELIGION$ patriarchs only
		ai_chance = { factor = 40 }
		if = {
			limit = {
				any_owned_province = {
					has_province_flag = orthodox_pentarchy
					has_owner_religion = no
					OR = {
						religion = orthodox
						religion = coptic
					}
				}
			}
			every_owned_province = {
				limit = {
					has_province_flag = orthodox_pentarchy
					has_owner_religion = no
					OR = {
						religion = orthodox
						religion = coptic
					}
				}
				hidden_effect = {
					set_variable = { which = added_unrest value = 10 }
					add_base_unrest = yes
				}
				custom_tooltip = added_unrest_10
			}
		}
		#People's reaction
		dg_add_prestige_small = yes
		if = {
			limit = { piety = 0.60 }
			add_adm_power = 20
			if = {
				limit = { NOT = { stability = 0 } }
				random = { chance = 25 add_stability_1 = yes }
			}
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = { piety = 0.20 }
			add_adm_power = 16
			if = {
				limit = { NOT = { stability = 0 } }
				random = { chance = 20 add_stability_1 = yes }
			}
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = { piety = -0.20 }
			add_adm_power = 12
			if = {
				limit = { NOT = { stability = 0 } }
				random = { chance = 15 add_stability_1 = yes }
			}
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = { piety = -0.60 }
			add_adm_power = 8
			if = {
				limit = { NOT = { stability = 0 } }
				random = { chance = 10 add_stability_1 = yes }
			}
		}
		else = {
			add_adm_power = 4
			if = {
				limit = { NOT = { stability = 0 } }
				random = { chance = 5 add_stability_1 = yes }
			}
		}
		#Church's reaction
		if = {
			limit = { patriarch_authority = 0.80 }
			add_legitimacy = 10
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = { patriarch_authority = 0.60 }
			add_legitimacy = 8
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = { patriarch_authority = 0.40 }
			add_legitimacy = 6
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = { patriarch_authority = 0.20 }
			add_legitimacy = 4
		}
		else = {
			add_legitimacy = 2
		}
		trigger_switch = {
			on_trigger = has_country_modifier
			unhappy_church_powerful = {
				remove_country_modifier = unhappy_church_powerful
			}
			unhappy_church_strong = {
				remove_country_modifier = unhappy_church_strong
			}
			unhappy_church_moderate = {
				remove_country_modifier = unhappy_church_moderate
			}
			unhappy_church_weak = {
				remove_country_modifier = unhappy_church_weak
			}
			unhappy_church_impotent = {
				remove_country_modifier = unhappy_church_impotent
			}
		}
		hidden_effect = { change_variable = { which = union_of_churches_state_support value = 1 } }
		if = {
			limit = { NOT = { check_variable = { which = miaphysite_council_topics value = 1 } } }
			country_event = { id = dg_miaphysite.015 days = 10 }
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = dg_miaphysite.012.b #Allow locals to decide
		ai_chance = { factor = 30 }
		hidden_effect = {
			every_owned_province = {
				limit = {
					has_province_flag = orthodox_pentarchy
					religion = orthodox
					has_owner_religion = yes
				}
				owner = { change_variable = { which = union_of_churches_state_support value = 0.25 } }
			}
			every_owned_province = {
				limit = {
					has_province_flag = orthodox_pentarchy
					religion = orthodox
					has_owner_religion = no
				}
				owner = { change_variable = { which = union_of_churches_minority_support value = 0.25 } }
			}
			every_owned_province = {
				limit = {
					has_province_flag = orthodox_pentarchy
					religion = coptic
					has_owner_religion = yes
				}
				owner = { change_variable = { which = union_of_churches_state_support value = 0.25 } }
			}
			every_owned_province = {
				limit = {
					has_province_flag = orthodox_pentarchy
					religion = coptic
					has_owner_religion = no
				}
				owner = { change_variable = { which = union_of_churches_minority_support value = 0.25 } }
			}
		}
		#People's reaction
		if = {
			limit = { piety = 0.60 }
			subtract_stability_1 = yes
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = { piety = 0.20 }
			random = { chance = 80 subtract_stability_1 = yes }
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = { piety = -0.20 }
			random = { chance = 60 subtract_stability_1 = yes }
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = { piety = -0.60 }
			random = { chance = 40 subtract_stability_1 = yes }
		}
		else = {
			random = { chance = 20 subtract_stability_1 = yes }
		}
		#Church's reaction
		if = {
			limit = {
				NOT = {
					num_of_owned_provinces_with = {
						has_province_flag = orthodox_pentarchy
						has_owner_religion = yes
						value = 3
					}
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = { patriarch_authority = 0.80 }
				add_country_modifier = { name = unhappy_church_powerful duration = 1000 }
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = { patriarch_authority = 0.60 }
				add_country_modifier = { name = unhappy_church_strong duration = 1000 }
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = { patriarch_authority = 0.40 }
				add_country_modifier = { name = unhappy_church_moderate duration = 1000 }
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = { patriarch_authority = 0.20 }
				add_country_modifier = { name = unhappy_church_weak duration = 1000 }
			}
			else = {
				add_country_modifier = { name = unhappy_church_impotent duration = 1000 }
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = { NOT = { check_variable = { which = miaphysite_council_topics value = 1 } } }
			country_event = { id = dg_miaphysite.015 days = 10 }
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = dg_miaphysite.012.c #Historical split
		trigger = { owns_rome_trigger = no }
		ai_chance = { factor = 30 }
		if = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					2530 = { religion = coptic }
					1402 = { religion = coptic }
				}
			}
			every_owned_province = {
				limit = {
					OR = {
						province_rome_trigger = yes
						province_constantinople_trigger = yes
					}
					religion = coptic
				}
				hidden_effect = {
					set_variable = { which = added_unrest value = 10 }
					add_base_unrest = yes
				}
				custom_tooltip = added_unrest_10
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					358 = { religion = orthodox }
					379 = { religion = orthodox }
					382 = { religion = orthodox }
				}
			}
			every_owned_province = {
				limit = {
					OR = {
						province_id = 358 # Al Iskandariyya
						province_id = 379 # Al Quds
						province_id = 382 # Dimashq
					}
					religion = coptic
				}
				hidden_effect = {
					set_variable = { which = added_unrest value = 10 }
					add_base_unrest = yes
				}
				custom_tooltip = added_unrest_10
			}
		}
		#People's reaction
		if = {
			limit = { piety = 0.60 }
			add_legitimacy = -20
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = { piety = 0.20 }
			add_legitimacy = -16
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = { piety = -0.20 }
			add_legitimacy = -12
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = { piety = -0.60 }
			add_legitimacy = -8
		}
		else = {
			add_legitimacy = -4
		}
		#Church's reaction
		if = {
			limit = { patriarch_authority = 0.80 }
			add_country_modifier = { name = religious_scandal_country_strong duration = 2000 }
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = { patriarch_authority = 0.60 }
			add_country_modifier = { name = religious_scandal_country_strong duration = 1000 }
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = { patriarch_authority = 0.40 }
			add_country_modifier = { name = religious_scandal_country duration = 2000 }
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = { patriarch_authority = 0.20 }
			add_country_modifier = { name = religious_scandal_country_weak duration = 2000 }
		}
		else = {
			add_country_modifier = { name = religious_scandal_country_weak duration = 1000 }
		}
		hidden_effect = { change_variable = { which = union_of_churches_minority_support value = 1 } }
		if = {
			limit = { NOT = { check_variable = { which = miaphysite_council_topics value = 1 } } }
			country_event = { id = dg_miaphysite.015 days = 10 }
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = dg_miaphysite.012.c2 #Historical split (Rome owned)
		trigger = { owns_rome_trigger = yes }
		ai_chance = { factor = 30 }
		if = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					2530 = { religion = coptic }
					1402 = { religion = coptic }
				}
			}
			every_owned_province = {
				limit = {
					OR = {
						province_rome_trigger = yes
						province_constantinople_trigger = yes
					}
					religion = coptic
				}
				hidden_effect = {
					set_variable = { which = added_unrest value = 10 }
					add_base_unrest = yes
				}
				custom_tooltip = added_unrest_10
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					358 = { religion = orthodox }
					379 = { religion = orthodox }
					382 = { religion = orthodox }
				}
			}
			every_owned_province = {
				limit = {
					OR = {
						province_id = 358 # Al Iskandariyya
						province_id = 379 # Al Quds
						province_id = 382 # Dimashq
					}
					religion = coptic
				}
				hidden_effect = {
					set_variable = { which = added_unrest value = 10 }
					add_base_unrest = yes
				}
				custom_tooltip = added_unrest_10
			}
		}
		#People's reaction
		if = {
			limit = { piety = 0.60 }
			subtract_stability_1 = yes
			add_legitimacy = -20
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = { piety = 0.20 }
			random = { chance = 80 subtract_stability_1 = yes }
			add_legitimacy = -16
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = { piety = -0.20 }
			random = { chance = 60 subtract_stability_1 = yes }
			add_legitimacy = -12
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = { piety = -0.60 }
			random = { chance = 40 subtract_stability_1 = yes }
			add_legitimacy = -8
		}
		else = {
			random = { chance = 20 subtract_stability_1 = yes }
			add_legitimacy = -4
		}
		#Church's reaction
		if = {
			limit = { patriarch_authority = 0.80 }
			add_country_modifier = { name = religious_scandal_country_strong duration = 2000 }
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = { patriarch_authority = 0.60 }
			add_country_modifier = { name = religious_scandal_country_strong duration = 1000 }
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = { patriarch_authority = 0.40 }
			add_country_modifier = { name = religious_scandal_country duration = 2000 }
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = { patriarch_authority = 0.20 }
			add_country_modifier = { name = religious_scandal_country_weak duration = 2000 }
		}
		else = {
			add_country_modifier = { name = religious_scandal_country_weak duration = 1000 }
		}

			limit = { NOT = { check_variable = { which = miaphysite_council_topics value = 1 } } }
			country_event = { id = dg_miaphysite.015 days = 10 }
		}
	}

country_event = { #The Question of Condemnation
	
	id = dg_miaphysite.013
	title = dg_miaphysite.013.t
	desc = dg_miaphysite.013.d
	picture = catholic_church_council
	
	trigger = {
		has_country_flag = miaphysite_council
		advisor = theologian
		check_variable = { which = miaphysite_council_topics value = 1 }
		NOT = { has_country_flag = miaphysite_agreement_condemnation }
	}
	
	mean_time_to_happen = {
		
		months = 25
		
		modifier = {
			OR = {
				has_country_modifier = unhappy_church_powerful
				has_country_modifier = unhappy_church_strong
				has_country_modifier = unhappy_church_moderate
				has_country_modifier = unhappy_church_weak
				has_country_modifier = unhappy_church_impotent
			}
			factor = 1.4
		}
		modifier = {
			OR = {
				has_country_modifier = religious_scandal_country_strong
				has_country_modifier = religious_scandal_country
				has_country_modifier = religious_scandal_country_weak
			}
			factor = 2
		}
		modifier = {
			theologian = 2
			factor = 0.7
		}
		modifier = {
			theologian = 3
			factor = 0.7
		}
		modifier = {
			has_country_modifier = union_of_churches
			factor = 0.5
		}
	}
	
	immediate = {
		clr_country_flag = miaphysite_council_falters
		hidden_effect = {
			change_variable = { which = miaphysite_council_topics value = -1 }
			set_country_flag = miaphysite_agreement_condemnation
			set_country_flag = miaphysite_agreement_ratification_needed
			if = {
				limit = { theologian = 3 }
				change_variable = { which = union_of_churches_minority_support value = 0.25 }
				change_variable = { which = union_of_churches_state_support value = 0.25 }
			}
			if = {
				limit = { theologian = 2 }
				change_variable = { which = union_of_churches_minority_support value = 0.25 }
				change_variable = { which = union_of_churches_state_support value = 0.25 }
			}
		}
	}
	
	option = {
		name = dg_miaphysite.013.a #$Let the dead rest
		ai_chance = { factor = 30 }
		#Church's reaction
		if = {
			limit = { patriarch_authority = 0.80 }
			add_legitimacy = 5
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = { patriarch_authority = 0.60 }
			add_legitimacy = 4
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = { patriarch_authority = 0.40 }
			add_legitimacy = 3
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = { patriarch_authority = 0.20 }
			add_legitimacy = 2
		}
		else = {
			add_legitimacy = 1
		}
		trigger_switch = {
			on_trigger = has_country_modifier
			unhappy_church_powerful = {
				remove_country_modifier = unhappy_church_powerful
			}
			unhappy_church_strong = {
				remove_country_modifier = unhappy_church_strong
			}
			unhappy_church_moderate = {
				remove_country_modifier = unhappy_church_moderate
			}
			unhappy_church_weak = {
				remove_country_modifier = unhappy_church_weak
			}
			unhappy_church_impotent = {
				remove_country_modifier = unhappy_church_impotent
			}
		}
		hidden_effect = { change_variable = { which = union_of_churches_state_support value = 0.5 } }
		if = {
			limit = { NOT = { check_variable = { which = miaphysite_council_topics value = 1 } } }
			country_event = { id = dg_miaphysite.015 days = 10 }
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = dg_miaphysite.013.b #Condemn the words, not the men
		ai_chance = { factor = 30 }
		#Church's reaction
		if = {
			limit = { patriarch_authority = 0.80 }

		}
		else_if = {
			limit = { patriarch_authority = 0.60 }
			add_country_modifier = { name = unhappy_church_strong duration = 1000 }
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = { patriarch_authority = 0.40 }
			add_country_modifier = { name = unhappy_church_moderate duration = 1000 }
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = { patriarch_authority = 0.20 }
			add_country_modifier = { name = unhappy_church_weak duration = 1000 }
		}
		else = {
			add_country_modifier = { name = unhappy_church_impotent duration = 1000 }
		}
		if = {
			limit = { NOT = { check_variable = { which = miaphysite_council_topics value = 1 } } }
			country_event = { id = dg_miaphysite.015 days = 10 }
		}
	}
	option = {

				random = { chance = 40 subtract_stability_1 = yes }
				add_legitimacy = -8
			}
			else = {
				random = { chance = 20 subtract_stability_1 = yes }
				add_legitimacy = -4
			}
			#Church's reaction
			if = {
				limit = { patriarch_authority = 0.80 }
				add_country_modifier = { name = religious_scandal_country_strong duration = 2000 }
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = { patriarch_authority = 0.60 }
				add_country_modifier = { name = religious_scandal_country_strong duration = 1000 }
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = { patriarch_authority = 0.40 }
				add_country_modifier = { name = religious_scandal_country duration = 2000 }
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = { patriarch_authority = 0.20 }
				add_country_modifier = { name = religious_scandal_country_weak duration = 2000 }
			}
			else = {
				add_country_modifier = { name = religious_scandal_country_weak duration = 1000 }
			}
			hidden_effect = { change_variable = { which = union_of_churches_state_support value = -2 } }
			if = {
				limit = { NOT = { check_variable = { which = miaphysite_council_topics value = 1 } } }
				country_event = { id = dg_miaphysite.015 days = 10 }
			}
		}
	}
}

country_event = { #15 - Act of Union
	
	id = dg_miaphysite.015
	title = dg_miaphysite.015.t
	desc = dg_miaphysite.015.d
	picture = orthodox_autocephaly
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	option = {
		name = dg_miaphysite.015.a
		hidden_effect = {
			regiongroup = {
				region = {
					limit = { has_province_flag = orthodox_pentarchy }
					set_province_flag = miaphysite_union
				}
			}
			if = { #If there are no concessions to the minority, they will reject it
				limit = { NOT = { check_variable = { which = union_of_churches_minority_support value = 1 } } }
				change_variable = { which = miaphysite_union_support value = -2 }
				set_country_flag = union_unfair_minority
			}
			#If one side has much more support than the other, the other will reject it
			multiply_variable = { which = union_of_churches_minority_support value = 2 }
			if = {
				limit = { check_variable = { which = union_of_churches_state_support which = union_of_churches_minority_support } }
				change_variable = { which = miaphysite_union_support value = -1.5 }
				set_country_flag = union_unfair_minority
			}
			multiply_variable = { which = union_of_churches_minority_support value = 0.5 }
			multiply_variable = { which = union_of_churches_state_support value = 2 }
			if = {
				limit = { check_variable = { which = union_of_churches_minority_support which = union_of_churches_state_support } }
				change_variable = { which = miaphysite_union_support value = -1.5 }
				set_country_flag = union_unfair_state
			}
			multiply_variable = { which = union_of_churches_state_support value = 0.5 }
		}
	}
}

	}
	
	mean_time_to_happen = {
		
		months = 5

			owner = { check_variable = { which = union_of_churches_minority_support which = union_of_churches_state_support } }
			factor = 0.5
		}
		modifier = {
			owner = { check_variable = { which = union_of_churches_state_support value = 1 } }
			factor = 1.4
		}
		modifier = {
			owner = { check_variable = { which = union_of_churches_state_support value = 2 } }
			factor = 1.4
		}
		modifier = {
			owner = { check_variable = { which = union_of_churches_state_support value = 3 } }
			factor = 1.4
		}
		modifier = {
			owner = { check_variable = { which = union_of_churches_state_support value = 4 } }
			factor = 1.4
		}
		modifier = {
			owner = { patriarch_authority = 0.80 }
			factor = 0.7
		}
		modifier = {
			owner = { patriarch_authority = 0.60 }
			factor = 0.7
		}
		modifier = {
			owner = { NOT = { patriarch_authority = 0.40 } }
			factor = 1.4
		}
		modifier = {
			owner = { NOT = { patriarch_authority = 0.20 } }
			factor = 1.4
		}
		modifier = {
			owner = { has_country_flag = patriarch_controversial }
			factor = 0.7
		}
		modifier = {

			factor = 0.5
		}
		modifier = {
			owner = { has_country_flag = patriarch_theologian }
			factor = 1.4
		}
		modifier = {
			owner = { has_country_flag = patriarch_obedient }
			factor = 2
		}
		modifier = {
			owner = { has_country_flag = patriarch_corrupt }
			factor = 2
		}
	}
	
	immediate = { clr_province_flag = miaphysite_union }
	
	option = {
		name = dg_miaphysite.016.a #Bribe him
		ai_chance = { factor = 50 }
		owner = {
			hidden_effect = { change_variable = { which = miaphysite_union_support value = 0.25 } }
			if = { #Maximum
				limit = { monthly_income = 250 }
				add_treasury = -250
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = { monthly_income = 10 }
				add_years_of_income = -0.08
			}
			else = { #Minimum
				add_treasury = -10
			}
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = dg_miaphysite.016.b #Put pressure on him
		ai_chance = { factor = 50 }
		owner = {
			hidden_effect = { change_variable = { which = miaphysite_union_support value = 0.25 } }
			if = {
				limit = { patriarch_authority = 0.80 }
				add_adm_power = -25
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = { patriarch_authority = 0.60 }
				add_adm_power = -20
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = { patriarch_authority = 0.40 }
				add_adm_power = -15
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = { patriarch_authority = 0.20 }
				add_adm_power = -10
			}
			else = {
				add_adm_power = -5
			}
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = dg_miaphysite.016.c #Accept his refusal
		owner = {
			hidden_effect = { change_variable = { which = miaphysite_union_support value = -1 } }
			if = {
				limit = { piety = 0.60 }
				add_prestige = -10
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = { piety = 0.20 }
				add_prestige = -8
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = { piety = -0.20 }
				add_prestige = -6
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = { piety = -0.60 }
				add_prestige = -4
			}
			else = {
				add_prestige = -2
			}
		}
	}
}

	}

	option = {

		}

			limit = { piety = 0.20 }
			add_prestige = -8
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = { piety = -0.20 }
			add_prestige = -6
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = { piety = -0.60 }
			add_prestige = -4
		}
		else = {
			add_prestige = -2
		}
		random_known_country = {
			limit = { has_country_flag = miaphysite_council }

			country_event = { id = dg_miaphysite.020 days = 30 }
		}
	}

country_event = { #21 - Union approved
	
	id = dg_miaphysite.021
	title = dg_miaphysite.021.t
	desc = dg_miaphysite.021.d
	picture = orthodox_metropolitan
	
	trigger = {
		has_country_flag = miaphysite_agreement
		NOT = { has_country_modifier = union_of_churches }
		NOT = { check_variable = { which = miaphysite_council_topics value = 1 } }
		NOT = { any_province = { has_province_flag = miaphysite_council } }
		check_variable = { which = miaphysite_union_support value = -0.5 }
	}

			check_variable = { which = miaphysite_union_support value = 1 }
			factor = 0.7

			check_variable = { which = miaphysite_union_support value = 2 }
			factor = 0.7
		}
		modifier = {
			check_variable = { which = miaphysite_union_support value = 3 }
			factor = 0.7
		}
		modifier = {
			check_variable = { which = miaphysite_union_support value = 4 }
			factor = 0.7
		}
	}
	
	immediate = {
		clr_country_flag = miaphysite_agreement
		clr_country_flag = miaphysite_council
		clr_country_flag = miaphysite_union
	}
	
	option = {
		name = dg_miaphysite.021.a
		if = {
			limit = { NOT = { has_country_modifier = union_of_churches } }

				limit = { piety = 0.60 }
				add_prestige = 10
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = { piety = 0.20 }
				add_prestige = 8
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = { piety = -0.20 }
				add_prestige = 6
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = { piety = -0.60 }
				add_prestige = 4
			}
			else = {
				add_prestige = 2
			}
			add_country_modifier = { name = union_of_churches duration = -1 }
		}
		if = {
			limit = { has_country_flag = miaphysite_agreement_language }
			set_country_flag = miaphysite_agreement_language_done
		}
		if = {
			limit = { has_country_flag = miaphysite_agreement_condemnation }
			set_country_flag = miaphysite_agreement_condemnation_done
		}
		if = {
			limit = { has_country_flag = miaphysite_agreement_patriarchs }
			set_country_flag = miaphysite_agreement_patriarchs_done
		}
		if = {
			limit = { has_country_flag = miaphysite_agreement_nature }
			set_country_flag = miaphysite_agreement_nature_done
		}
		hidden_effect = { set_variable = { which = miaphysite_union_support value = 0 } }
	}
}

		clr_country_flag = miaphysite_council

			clr_country_flag = miaphysite_agreement_patriarchs
		}
		if = {
			limit = { NOT = { has_country_flag = miaphysite_agreement_nature_done } }
			clr_country_flag = miaphysite_agreement_nature
		}
	}
	
	option = {
		name = dg_miaphysite.021.a
		clr_country_flag = miaphysite_union
		if = {
			limit = { piety = 0.60 }
			add_prestige = -10
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = { piety = 0.20 }
			add_prestige = -8
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = { piety = -0.20 }
			add_prestige = -6
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = { piety = -0.60 }
			add_prestige = -4
		}
		else = {
			add_prestige = -2
		}
		hidden_effect = { set_variable = { which = miaphysite_union_support value = 0 } }
	}
}

country_event = { #23 - True Union of the Churches
	
	id = dg_miaphysite.023

	desc = dg_miaphysite.023.d
	picture = orthodox_autocephaly

		NOT = { check_variable = { which = miaphysite_council_topics value = 1 } }
		NOT = { any_province = { has_province_flag = miaphysite_council } }
		check_variable = { which = miaphysite_union_support value = -0.5 }
	}
	
	mean_time_to_happen = {
		
		months = 25
		
		modifier = {
			check_variable = { which = miaphysite_union_support value = 1 }
			factor = 0.7
		}
		modifier = {
			check_variable = { which = miaphysite_union_support value = 2 }
			factor = 0.7
		}
		modifier = {
			check_variable = { which = miaphysite_union_support value = 3 }
			factor = 0.7
		}
		modifier = {
			check_variable = { which = miaphysite_union_support value = 4 }
			factor = 0.7
		}
	}
	
	immediate = {
		clr_country_flag = miaphysite_agreement
		if = {
			limit = { religion = orthodox }
			custom_tooltip = chaldean_holdouts
		}
		if = {
			limit = { religion = coptic }
			custom_tooltip = gnostic_holdouts
		}
	}
	
	option = {
		name = dg_miaphysite.023.a
		if = {
			limit = { religion = orthodox }
			set_global_flag = miaphysite_orthodox_union
		}
		if = {
			limit = { religion = coptic }
			set_global_flag = orthodox_miaphysite_union
		}
		remove_country_modifier = union_of_churches
		set_country_flag = support_miaphysite_union
		if = {
			limit = { piety = 0.60 }
			add_prestige = 50
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = { piety = 0.20 }
			add_prestige = 40
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = { piety = -0.20 }
			add_prestige = 30
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = { piety = -0.60 }
			add_prestige = 20
		}
		else = {
			add_prestige = 10
		}

			if = {
				limit = { religion = orthodox }
				every_owned_province = {
					limit = { check_variable = { which = coptic value = 4 } }
					change_variable = { which = converts value = 3 }

				}

					}

				}

					limit = {

					}

			set_variable = { which = miaphysite_union_state_support value = 0 }
			country_event = { id = dg_conversion.001 }
		}
	}

				has_global_flag = orthodox_miaphysite_union
				religion = orthodox
			}
			change_religion = gnostic
			hidden_effect = {
				every_owned_province = {
					limit = { check_variable = { which = orthodox value = 4 } }
					set_province_flag = religious_change
					change_variable = { which = coptic value = 1 }
					change_variable = { which = gnostic value = 3 }
					change_variable = { which = orthodox value = -4 }
				}
				every_owned_province = {
					limit = { check_variable = { which = orthodox value = 4 } }
					change_variable = { which = coptic value = 1 }
					change_variable = { which = gnostic value = 3 }
					change_variable = { which = orthodox value = -4 }
				}
				every_owned_province = {
					limit = { check_variable = { which = orthodox value = 4 } }
					change_variable = { which = coptic value = 1 }
					change_variable = { which = gnostic value = 3 }
					change_variable = { which = orthodox value = -4 }
				}
				every_owned_province = {
					limit = { check_variable = { which = orthodox value = 4 } }
					change_variable = { which = coptic value = 1 }
					change_variable = { which = gnostic value = 3 }
					change_variable = { which = orthodox value = -4 }
				}
				every_owned_province = {
					limit = { check_variable = { which = orthodox value = 4 } }
					change_variable = { which = coptic value = 1 }
					change_variable = { which = gnostic value = 3 }
					change_variable = { which = orthodox value = -4 }
				}
				every_owned_province = {
					limit = { check_variable = { which = orthodox value = 2 } }
					change_variable = { which = orthodox value = -2 }
					set_province_flag = religious_change
					random_list = {
						75 = { change_variable = { which = gnostic value = 2 } }
						25 = { change_variable = { which = coptic value = 2 } }
					}
				}
			}
		}
	}
}

country_event = { #31 - A Visit by the Catholicos
	
	id = dg_miaphysite.031
	title = dg_miaphysite.031.t
	desc = dg_miaphysite.031.d
	picture = orthodox_patriarch_migration
	
	trigger = {
		religion = coptic
		OR = {
			AND = { #Alexandria (Ecumenical?)
				capital_scope = { NOT = { continent = europe } }
				alexandria_patriarch_area = {
					has_province_flag = miaphysite_catholicos_of_alexandria
					OR = {
						has_province_modifier = coptic_patriarchate_captive
						has_province_modifier = coptic_patriarchate_vacant
					}
					owner = { NOT = { religion = coptic } }
				}
			}
			AND = { #Antioch and Europe (?)
				capital_scope = { continent = europe }
				antioch_patriarch_area = {
					has_province_flag = miaphysite_catholicos_of_antioch
					OR = {
						has_province_modifier = coptic_patriarchate_captive
						has_province_modifier = coptic_patriarchate_vacant
					}
					owner = { NOT = { religion = coptic } }
				}
			}
		}
	}
	
	mean_time_to_happen = {
		
		years = 41
		
		modifier = {
			any_owned_province = { has_province_modifier = coptic_patriarchate }
			factor = 3
		}
		modifier = {
			piety = 0.60
			factor = 0.7
		}
		modifier = {
			piety = 0.20
			factor = 0.7
		}
		modifier = {
			NOT = { piety = -0.20 }
			factor = 1.4
		}
		modifier = {
			NOT = { piety = -0.60 }
			factor = 1.4
		}
		modifier = {
			patriarch_authority = 0.80
			NOT = { any_owned_province = { has_province_modifier = coptic_patriarchate } }
			factor = 0.7
		}
		modifier = {
			patriarch_authority = 0.60
			NOT = { any_owned_province = { has_province_modifier = coptic_patriarchate } }
			factor = 0.7
		}
		modifier = {
			NOT = { patriarch_authority = 0.40 }
			factor = 1.4
		}
		modifier = {
			NOT = { patriarch_authority = 0.20 }
			factor = 1.4
		}
	}
	
	option = {
		name = dg_orthodox.021.a #Collect a tithe for our brethren
		ai_chance = { factor = 60 }
		if = {
			limit = { monthly_income = 500 }
			add_treasury = -500
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = { monthly_income = 5 }
			add_years_of_income = -0.08
		}
		else = {
			add_treasury = -5
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = dg_orthodox.021.b #Promise to regain his lost seat
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 20
			modifier = {
				num_of_cities = 8
				factor = 1.4
			}
			modifier = {
				num_of_cities = 12
				factor = 1.4
			}
			modifier = {
				num_of_cities = 20
				factor = 1.4
			}
			modifier = {
				num_of_cities = 30
				factor = 1.4
			}
			modifier = {
				num_of_cities = 40
				factor = 1.4
			}
		}
		trigger = {
			piety = 0.20
			is_free_or_tributary_trigger = yes
			OR = {
				AND = {
					capital_scope = { continent = europe }
					antioch_patriarch_area = {
						has_province_flag = miaphysite_catholicos_of_antioch
						NOT = { has_province_flag = miaphysite_catholicate_of_antioch }
					}
				}
				AND = {
					capital_scope = { NOT = { continent = europe } }
					alexandria_patriarch_area = {
						has_province_flag = miaphysite_catholicos_of_alexandria
						NOT = { has_province_flag = miaphysite_catholicate_of_alexandria }
					}
				}
			}
		}
		add_dip_power = -25
		if = {
			limit = { capital_scope = { continent = europe } }
			antioch_patriarch_area = {
				limit = {
					has_province_flag = miaphysite_catholicos_of_antioch
				}
				owner = { reverse_add_casus_belli = { type = cb_holy_war_vengeance target = ROOT months = 60 } }
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = { capital_scope = { NOT = { continent = europe } } }
			alexandria_patriarch_area = {
				limit = {
					has_province_flag = miaphysite_catholicos_of_alexandria
				}
				owner = { reverse_add_casus_belli = { type = cb_holy_war_vengeance target = ROOT months = 60 } }
			}
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = dg_orthodox.021.c #Offer him our prayers
		ai_chance = { factor = 20 }
		if = {
			limit = { piety = 0.60 }
			add_prestige = -8
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = { piety = 0.20 }
			add_prestige = -6
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = { piety = -0.20 }
			add_prestige = -4
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = { piety = -0.60 }
			add_prestige = -2
		}
	}
}

province_event = { #32 - Fate of the Catholicate
	
	id = dg_miaphysite.032
	title = dg_miaphysite.032.t
	desc = dg_miaphysite.032.d
	picture = orthodox_metropolitan
	
	trigger = {
		has_province_flag = coptic_patriarchate
		NOT = { has_province_modifier = coptic_patriarchate_vacant }
		NOT = { has_province_modifier = coptic_patriarchate_captive }
		NOT = { has_province_modifier = catholic_patriarchate }
		OR = {
			NOT = { owner = { religion = catholic } }
			province_rome_trigger = no
		}
		NOT = { owner = { religion = coptic } }
		controlled_by = owner
	}
	
	mean_time_to_happen = { months = 5 }
	
	immediate = {
		remove_province_modifier = coptic_patriarchate
		remove_province_modifier = coptic_archbishopric
		remove_province_modifier = coptic_pentarchy
		hidden_effect = {
			every_province = {
				limit = { region = ROOT }
				if = {
					limit = { check_variable = { which = coptic value = 10 } }
					PREV = { change_variable = { which = patriarch_influence value = 5 } }
				}
				else_if = {
					limit = { check_variable = { which = coptic value = 8 } }
					PREV = { change_variable = { which = patriarch_influence value = 4 } }
				}
				else_if = {
					limit = { check_variable = { which = coptic value = 6 } }
					PREV = { change_variable = { which = patriarch_influence value = 3 } }
				}
				else_if = {
					limit = { check_variable = { which = coptic value = 4 } }
					PREV = { change_variable = { which = patriarch_influence value = 2 } }
				}
				else_if = {
					limit = { check_variable = { which = coptic value = 2 } }
					PREV = { change_variable = { which = patriarch_influence value = 1 } }
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					any_province = {
						region = ROOT
						NOT = { province_id = ROOT }
						OR = {
							has_province_modifier = coptic_patriarchate
							has_province_modifier = coptic_archbishopric
							has_province_modifier = coptic_patriarchate_captive
						}
					}
				}
				multiply_variable = { which = patriarch_influence value = 0.7 }
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					any_province = {
						region = ROOT
						NOT = { province_id = ROOT }
						has_province_flag = coptic_pentarchy
					}
				}
				multiply_variable = { which = patriarch_influence value = 0.7 }
			}
		}
	}
	
	option = {
		name = dg_miaphysite.032.e #Reaffirm the current Patriarch
		trigger = {
			OR = {
				owner = { religion_group = christian }
				owner = { has_country_flag = christians_tolerated }
			}
		}
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 25
			modifier = {
				NOT = { religion_group = christian }
				owner = { religion_group = christian }
				factor = 2
			}
			modifier = {
				NOT = { check_variable = { which = patriarch_influence value = 10 } }
				factor = 2
			}
		}
		owner = {
			add_country_modifier = { name = religious_controversy duration = 500 }
			every_known_country = {
				limit = { religion = coptic }
				add_opinion = { who = ROOT modifier = recognized_current_patriarch }
			}
		}
		add_province_modifier = { name = coptic_patriarchate_captive duration = -1 }
		hidden_effect = { set_variable = { which = patriarch_influence value = 0 } }
	}
	option = {
		name = dg_miaphysite.032.a #Appoint a loyal Patriarch
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 25
			modifier = {
				owner = {
					any_owned_province = {
						culture = ROOT
						religion = coptic
						NOT = { is_core = owner }
					}
				}
				factor = 2
			}
		}
		owner = {
			every_owned_province = {
				limit = {
					OR = {
						religion = coptic
						province_id = ROOT
					}
					region = ROOT
				}
				add_nationalism = -3
			}
		}
		add_province_modifier = { name = coptic_patriarchate_captive duration = -1 }
		hidden_effect = { set_variable = { which = patriarch_influence value = 0 } }
	}
	option = {
		name = dg_orthodox.022.b #Demand a tithe in return for the right
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 25
			modifier = {
				owner = { num_of_loans = 1 }
				factor = 1.4
			}
			modifier = {
				owner = { num_of_loans = 3 }
				factor = 1.4
			}
			modifier = {
				owner = { is_bankrupt = yes }
				factor = 2
			}
			modifier = {
				owner = { NOT = { treasury = 50 } }
				factor = 1.4
			}
			modifier = {
				owner = { NOT = { treasury = 100 } }
				factor = 1.4
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = { check_variable = { which = patriarch_influence value = 24 } }
			owner = { add_treasury = 50 }
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = { check_variable = { which = patriarch_influence value = 18 } }
			owner = { add_treasury = 40 }
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = { check_variable = { which = patriarch_influence value = 12 } }
			owner = { add_treasury = 30 }
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = { check_variable = { which = patriarch_influence value = 6 } }
			owner = { add_treasury = 20 }
		}
		else = {
			owner = { add_treasury = 10 }
		}
		add_province_modifier = { name = coptic_patriarchate_captive duration = -1 }
		hidden_effect = { set_variable = { which = patriarch_influence value = 0 } }
	}
	option = {
		name = dg_miaphysite.032.c #Close down the patriarchate and confiscate its property
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 25
			modifier = {
				owner = { num_of_loans = 1 }
				factor = 1.4
			}
			modifier = {
				owner = { num_of_loans = 3 }
				factor = 1.4
			}
			modifier = {
				owner = { is_bankrupt = yes }
				factor = 2
			}
			modifier = {
				owner = { NOT = { treasury = 100 } }
				factor = 1.4
			}
			modifier = {
				owner = { NOT = { treasury = 250 } }
				factor = 1.4
			}
			modifier = {
				owner = { has_country_flag = christians_tolerated }
				factor = 0.25
			}
			modifier = {
				owner = { has_country_flag = christians_permitted }
				factor = 0.5
			}
			modifier = {
				owner = {
					any_owned_province = {
						has_province_modifier = coptic_patriarchate_captive
						culture = ROOT
					}
				}
				factor = 5
			}
			modifier = {
				owner = { check_variable = { which = coptic_population value = 10 } }
				factor = 0.5
			}
			modifier = {
				owner = { check_variable = { which = coptic_population value = 20 } }
				factor = 0.5
			}
			modifier = {
				owner = { check_variable = { which = coptic_population value = 30 } }
				factor = 0.5
			}
			modifier = {
				owner = { check_variable = { which = coptic_population value = 40 } }
				factor = 0
			}
		}
		trigger = {
			owner = { NOT = { coptic = 2 } }
			owner = { NOT = { has_country_flag = useful_coptic } }
			owner = { NOT = { has_country_flag = useful_coptic } }
		}
		if = {
			limit = { check_variable = { which = patriarch_influence value = 24 } }
			owner = { add_treasury = 250 }
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = { check_variable = { which = patriarch_influence value = 18 } }
			owner = { add_treasury = 200 }
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = { check_variable = { which = patriarch_influence value = 12 } }
			owner = { add_treasury = 150 }
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = { check_variable = { which = patriarch_influence value = 6 } }
			owner = { add_treasury = 100 }
		}
		else = {
			owner = { add_treasury = 50 }
		}
		owner = {
			every_owned_province = {
				limit = {
					OR = {
						religion = coptic
						province_id = ROOT
					}
					region = ROOT
				}
				hidden_effect = {
					set_variable = { which = added_unrest value = 5 }
					add_base_unrest = yes
				}
				custom_tooltip = added_unrest_5
				add_nationalism = 5
			}
		}
		hidden_effect = { add_permanent_province_modifier = { name = coptic_patriarchate_vacant duration = -1 } }
		hidden_effect = { set_variable = { which = patriarch_influence value = 0 } }
	}
}

province_event = { #23 - Recovery of $PROVINCECAPITAL$

	desc = dg_miaphysite.033.d

	trigger = {
		has_province_flag = coptic_patriarchate

		NOT = { has_province_modifier = coptic_pentarchy }

	}
	
	mean_time_to_happen = { months = 5 }
	
	immediate = {
		remove_province_modifier = coptic_patriarchate_vacant
		remove_province_modifier = coptic_patriarchate_captive
	}

		name = dg_miaphysite.033.a #Appoint the new patriarch
		trigger = {

				limit = { piety = 0.60 }

			}

				}
			}

				limit = {
					alexandria_patriarch_area = {
						has_province_flag = miaphysite_catholicos_of_alexandria
						province_id = ROOT
					}
				}
				every_country = {
					limit = {
						religion = coptic
						capital_scope = { NOT = { continent = europe } NOT = { continent = mena } }
						NOT = { tag = ROOT }
					}
					country_event = { id = dg_miaphysite.038 days = 30 }
				}
			}
		}
		else = {
			every_country = {
				limit = {
					religion = coptic
					primary_culture = PREV
					NOT = { tag = ROOT }
				}
				country_event = { id = dg_miaphysite.038 days = 30 }
			}
		}
	}

		name = dg_miaphysite.033.c #Appoint a new patriarch
		trigger = {

				owner = { any_owned_province = { has_province_modifier = coptic_patriarchate } }

			}
		}

				if = {

					add_prestige = 4
				}
				else_if = {
					limit = { piety = 0.20 }
					add_prestige = 3
				}
				else_if = {
					limit = { piety = -0.20 }
					add_prestige = 2
				}
				else_if = {
					limit = { piety = -0.60 }
					add_prestige = 1
				}
			}
			add_province_modifier = { name = coptic_archbishopric duration = -1 }
		}

			limit = { has_province_flag = coptic_pentarchy }

					add_prestige = 8

					add_prestige = 6
				}
				else_if = {

				}
				else_if = {

					add_prestige = 2
				}
			}
			add_province_modifier = { name = coptic_pentarchy duration = -1 }
			if = {
				limit = { has_province_flag = coptic_pentarchy }

							has_province_flag = miaphysite_catholicos_of_antioch

							has_province_flag = miaphysite_catholicos_of_alexandria
							province_id = ROOT
						}

					}
				}
			}
		}
		else = {
			every_country = {
				limit = {
					religion = coptic
					primary_culture = PREV
					NOT = { tag = ROOT }
				}
				country_event = { id = dg_miaphysite.038 days = 30 }
			}
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = dg_orthodox.023.f #Place the $PROVINCECULTURE$ Church under the authority of $CAPITAL$
		trigger = {
			OR = {
				NOT = { culture_group = owner }
				AND = {
					has_owner_culture = yes
					owner = { any_owned_province = { has_owner_culture = yes has_province_modifier = coptic_patriarchate } }
				}
			}
			NOT = { has_province_flag = welcomed_refugee_patriarch }
			owner = {
				any_owned_province = {
					has_province_modifier = coptic_patriarchate
					OR = {
						has_owner_culture = yes
						is_capital = yes
						has_province_flag = coptic_pentarchy
					}
				}
			}
			NOT = { has_province_flag = coptic_pentarchy }
		}
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 50
			modifier = {
				OR = {
					AND = {
						owner = { total_development = 1200 }
						culture_group = owner
					}
					has_owner_accepted_culture = yes
				}
				factor = 0.5
			}
		}
		owner = {
			if = {
				limit = { piety = 0.60 }
				add_prestige = 16
				add_devotion = 16
				add_legitimacy = 8
				add_republican_tradition = 4
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = { piety = 0.20 }
				add_prestige = 12
				add_devotion = 12
				add_legitimacy = 6
				add_republican_tradition = 3
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = { piety = -0.20 }
				add_prestige = 8
				add_devotion = 8
				add_legitimacy = 4
				add_republican_tradition = 2
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = { piety = -0.60 }
				add_prestige = 4
				add_devotion = 4
				add_legitimacy = 2
				add_republican_tradition = 1
			}
		}
		clr_province_flag = welcomed_refugee_patriarch
		clr_province_flag = coptic_patriarchate
		hidden_effect = { add_permanent_province_modifier = { name = coptic_patriarchate_vacant duration = -1 } }
	}
	option = {
		name = dg_miaphysite.033.a #Appoint a new patriarch for $COUNTRY$
		trigger = {
			has_owner_culture = yes
			is_in_capital_area = yes
			owner = { is_free_or_tributary_trigger = yes }
			NOT = { has_province_flag = coptic_pentarchy }
			owner = { any_owned_province = { has_province_modifier = coptic_patriarchate } }
		}
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 25
			modifier = {
				is_capital = yes
				factor = 2
			}
			modifier = {
				owner = { has_country_flag = patriarch_corrupt }
				factor = 2
			}
			modifier = {
				owner = { has_country_flag = patriarch_controversial }
				factor = 1.4
			}
			modifier = {
				owner = { has_country_flag = patriarch_hostile }
				factor = 3
			}
			modifier = {
				owner = { has_country_flag = patriarch_obedient }
				factor = 0.5
			}
			modifier = {
				owner = { capital_scope = { has_province_modifier = coptic_patriarchate } }
				factor = 0
			}
			modifier = {
				owner = {
					any_owned_province = {
						has_province_modifier = coptic_patriarchate
						has_owner_culture = no
					}
				}
				factor = 2
			}
			modifier = {
				owner = {
					any_owned_province = {
						has_province_modifier = coptic_patriarchate
						NOT = { culture_group = owner }
					}
				}
				factor = 2
			}
		}
		owner = {
			if = {
				limit = { piety = 0.60 }
				add_prestige = 4
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = { piety = 0.20 }
				add_prestige = 3
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = { piety = -0.20 }
				add_prestige = 2
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = { piety = -0.60 }
				add_prestige = 1
			}
		}
		clr_province_flag = welcomed_refugee_patriarch
		owner = {
			if = {
				limit = { any_owned_province = { has_province_modifier = coptic_patriarchate } }
				every_owned_province = {
					limit = { has_province_modifier = coptic_patriarchate }
					remove_province_modifier = coptic_patriarchate
					if = {
						limit = { has_province_flag = coptic_pentarchy }
						add_province_modifier = { name = coptic_pentarchy duration = -1 }
					}
					else = {
						add_province_modifier = { name = coptic_archbishopric duration = -1 }
					}
				}
			}
		}
		add_province_modifier = { name = coptic_patriarchate duration = -1 }
		if = {
			limit = { owner = { NOT = { government = theocracy } } }
			province_event = { id = dg_miaphysite.036 }
		}
		if = {
			limit = { has_province_flag = coptic_pentarchy }
			if = {
				limit = {
					antioch_patriarch_area = {
						has_province_flag = miaphysite_catholicos_of_antioch
						province_id = ROOT
					}
				}
				every_country = {
					limit = {
						religion = coptic
						capital_scope = { continent = europe }
						NOT = { tag = ROOT }
					}
					country_event = { id = dg_miaphysite.038 days = 30 }
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					alexandria_patriarch_area = {
						has_province_flag = miaphysite_catholicos_of_alexandria
						province_id = ROOT
					}
				}
				every_country = {
					limit = {
						religion = coptic
						capital_scope = { NOT = { continent = europe } NOT = { continent = mena } }
						NOT = { tag = ROOT }
					}
					country_event = { id = dg_miaphysite.038 days = 30 }
				}
			}
		}
		else = {
			every_country = {
				limit = {
					religion = coptic
					primary_culture = PREV
					NOT = { tag = ROOT }
				}
				country_event = { id = dg_miaphysite.038 days = 30 }
			}
		}
	}
}

country_event = { #34 - The Patriarch of $COUNTRY$
	
	id = dg_miaphysite.034
	title = dg_miaphysite.034.t
	desc = dg_miaphysite.034.d
	picture = orthodox_metropolitan
	
	trigger = {
		religion = coptic
		NOT = { government = theocracy }
		NOT = { any_owned_province = { has_province_modifier = coptic_patriarchate } }
		any_owned_province = {
			OR = {
				has_province_modifier = coptic_archbishopric
				has_province_modifier = coptic_pentarchy
			}
		}
		is_free_or_tributary_trigger = yes
	}
	
	mean_time_to_happen = { months = 5 }
	
	immediate = {
		hidden_effect = {
			every_owned_province = {
				limit = { has_province_flag = coptic_patriarchate }
				if = {
					limit = { has_owner_culture = yes }
					change_variable = { which = patriarchate_seat value = 1 }
				}
				if = {
					limit = { culture_group = owner }
					change_variable = { which = patriarchate_seat value = 1 }
				}
				if = {
					limit = { is_core = owner }
					change_variable = { which = patriarchate_seat value = 1 }
				}
				if = {
					limit = { is_in_capital_area = yes }
					change_variable = { which = patriarchate_seat value = 1 }
				}
				if = {
					limit = { is_overseas = no } #Territory
					change_variable = { which = patriarchate_seat value = 1 }
				}
				if = {
					limit = { is_capital = yes }
					change_variable = { which = patriarchate_seat value = 1 }
				}
				if = {
					limit = { has_province_flag = coptic_pentarchy }
					change_variable = { which = patriarchate_seat value = 1 }
				}
			}
		}
	}
	
	option = {
		name = dg_orthodox.024.a #Excellent
		random_owned_province = {
			limit = {
				has_province_flag = coptic_patriarchate
				all_province = {
					has_province_flag = coptic_patriarchate
					owned_by = ROOT
					OR = {
						NOT = { check_variable = { which = patriarchate_seat which = PREV } }
						is_variable_equal = { which = patriarchate_seat which = PREV }
					}
				}
			}
			remove_province_modifier = coptic_archbishopric
			remove_province_modifier = coptic_pentarchy
			add_province_modifier = { name = coptic_patriarchate duration = -1 }
			province_event = { id = dg_miaphysite.036 }
		}
		hidden_effect = { every_owned_province = { set_variable = { which = patriarchate_seat value = 0 } } }
	}
}

country_event = { #A New Metropolitan
	
	id = dg_miaphysite.035
	title = dg_orthodox.025.t
	desc = dg_miaphysite.035.d
	picture = orthodox_patriarch_migration #TEMP
	
	trigger = {
		religion = coptic
		NOT = { any_owned_province = { has_province_modifier = coptic_patriarchate } }
		NOT = { government = theocracy }
		piety = -0.60
	}
	
	mean_time_to_happen = {
		
		years = 29
		
		modifier = {
			NOT = { has_country_flag = patriarch_appointed }
			factor = 0.35
		}
	}
	
	immediate = {
		clr_country_flag = patriarch_appointed
		set_country_flag = patriarch_appointed
		clr_country_flag = clerical_advisor
		clr_country_flag = patriarch_zealous
		clr_country_flag = patriarch_theologian
		clr_country_flag = patriarch_obedient
		clr_country_flag = patriarch_controversial
		clr_country_flag = patriarch_corrupt
		clr_country_flag = patriarch_hostile
		clr_country_flag = rival_patriarchs
		clr_country_flag = request_for_catholicos
		clr_country_flag = bribe_for_catholicos
	}
	
	option = {
		name = dg_orthodox.025.a #Ask for a new metropolitan to be appointed
		if = {
			limit = {
				overlord = {
					religion = coptic
					any_owned_province = {
						OR = {
							has_province_modifier = coptic_patriarchate
							has_province_modifier = coptic_pentarchy
							has_province_modifier = coptic_archbishopric
						}
					}
				}
			}
			overlord = {
				country_event = { id = dg_miaphysite.037 days = 30 }
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				NOT = {
					overlord = {
						religion = coptic
						any_owned_province = {
							OR = {
								has_province_modifier = coptic_patriarchate
								has_province_modifier = coptic_pentarchy
								has_province_modifier = coptic_archbishopric
							}
						}
					}
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					capital_scope = { continent = europe }
					antioch_patriarch_area = {
						has_province_flag = miaphysite_catholicos_of_antioch
						owner = { religion = coptic }
					}
				}
				antioch_patriarch_area = {
					limit = {
						has_province_flag = miaphysite_catholicos_of_antioch
					}
					owner = { country_event = { id = dg_miaphysite.037 days = 30 } }
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					capital_scope = { NOT = { continent = europe } }
					alexandria_patriarch_area = {
						has_province_flag = miaphysite_catholicos_of_alexandria
						owner = { religion = coptic }
					}
				}
				alexandria_patriarch_area = {
					limit = {
						has_province_flag = miaphysite_catholicos_of_alexandria
					}
					owner = { country_event = { id = dg_miaphysite.037 days = 30 } }
				}
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				NOT = {
					OR = {
						AND = { #Antioch and Europe
							capital_scope = { continent = europe }
							antioch_patriarch_area = {
								has_province_flag = miaphysite_catholicos_of_antioch
								owner = {
									religion = coptic
									OR = { ai = yes has_country_flag = religious_news_trivial }
								}
								OR = {
									has_province_modifier = coptic_patriarchate
									has_province_modifier = coptic_pentarchy
									has_province_modifier = coptic_archbishopric
								}
							}
						}
						AND = { #Alexandria
							capital_scope = { NOT = { continent = europe } }
							alexandria_patriarch_area = {
								has_province_flag = miaphysite_catholicos_of_alexandria
								owner = {
									religion = coptic
									OR = { ai = yes has_country_flag = religious_news_trivial }
								}
								OR = {
									has_province_modifier = coptic_patriarchate
									has_province_modifier = coptic_pentarchy
									has_province_modifier = coptic_archbishopric
								}
							}
						}
						overlord = {
							religion = coptic
							OR = { ai = yes has_country_flag = religious_news_trivial }
							any_owned_province = {
								OR = {
									has_province_modifier = coptic_patriarchate
									has_province_modifier = coptic_pentarchy
									has_province_modifier = coptic_archbishopric
								}
							}
						}
					}
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					overlord = {
						religion = coptic
						ai = no
						NOT = { has_country_flag = religious_news_trivial }
						any_owned_province = {
							OR = {
								has_province_modifier = coptic_patriarchate
								has_province_modifier = coptic_pentarchy
								has_province_modifier = coptic_archbishopric
							}
						}
					}
				}
				country_event = { id = dg_miaphysite.049 days = 60 }
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					NOT = {
						overlord = {
							religion = coptic
							ai = no
							NOT = { has_country_flag = religious_news_trivial }
							any_owned_province = {
								OR = {
									has_province_modifier = coptic_patriarchate
									has_province_modifier = coptic_pentarchy
									has_province_modifier = coptic_archbishopric
								}
							}
						}
					}
				}
				if = {
					limit = { capital_scope = { continent = europe } }
					if = {
						limit = {
							antioch_patriarch_area = {
								has_province_flag = miaphysite_catholicos_of_antioch
								owner = { religion = coptic }
							}
						}
						country_event = { id = dg_miaphysite.049 days = 60 }
					}
					if = {
						limit = {
							antioch_patriarch_area = {
								has_province_flag = miaphysite_catholicos_of_antioch
								owner = { NOT = { religion = coptic } }
							}
						}
						random_list = {
							30 = { country_event = { id = dg_miaphysite.047 days = 60 } }
							70 = { country_event = { id = dg_miaphysite.049 days = 60 } }
						}
					}
				}
				if = {
					limit = { capital_scope = { NOT = { continent = europe } } }
					if = {
						limit = {
							alexandria_patriarch_area = {
								has_province_flag = miaphysite_catholicos_of_alexandria
								owner = { religion = coptic }
							}
						}
						country_event = { id = dg_miaphysite.049 days = 60 }
					}
					if = {
						limit = {
							alexandria_patriarch_area = {
								has_province_flag = miaphysite_catholicos_of_alexandria
								owner = { NOT = { religion = coptic } }
							}
						}
						random_list = {
							30 = { country_event = { id = dg_miaphysite.047 days = 60 } }
							70 = { country_event = { id = dg_miaphysite.049 days = 60 } }
						}
					}
				}
			}
		}
	}
	after = {
		dg_patriarch_triggers = yes
	}
}

province_event = { #36 - The Catholicos of $PROVINCECAPITAL$ and All $COUNTRY$
	
	id = dg_miaphysite.036
	title = dg_miaphysite.036.t
	desc = dg_miaphysite.036.d
	picture = orthodox_metropolitan
	
	trigger = {
		has_province_modifier = coptic_patriarchate
		owner = { religion = coptic }
		owner = { NOT = { government = theocracy } }
		NOT = { owner = { has_country_flag = patriarchate_vacant } }
	}
	
	mean_time_to_happen = {
		
		years = 29
		
		modifier = {
			NOT = { owner = { has_country_flag = patriarch_appointed } }
			factor = 0.35
		}
	}
	
	immediate = {
		owner = {
			hidden_effect = {
				if = {
					limit = { has_country_flag = patriarch_hostile }
					set_variable = { which = patriarch_hostility value = 2 }
				}
				if = {
					limit = { has_country_flag = patriarch_controversial }
					set_variable = { which = patriarch_hostility value = 1 }
				}
			}
			clr_country_flag = patriarch_appointed
			set_country_flag = patriarch_appointed
			clr_country_flag = clerical_advisor
			clr_country_flag = patriarch_zealous
			clr_country_flag = patriarch_theologian
			clr_country_flag = patriarch_obedient
			clr_country_flag = patriarch_controversial
			clr_country_flag = patriarch_corrupt
			clr_country_flag = patriarch_hostile
			clr_country_flag = rival_patriarchs
			if = {
				limit = { has_country_modifier = unhappy_church_impotent }
				random = { chance = 60 remove_country_modifier = unhappy_church_impotent }
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = { has_country_modifier = unhappy_church_weak }
				random = { chance = 50 remove_country_modifier = unhappy_church_weak }
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = { has_country_modifier = unhappy_church_moderate }
				random = { chance = 40 remove_country_modifier = unhappy_church_moderate }
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = { has_country_modifier = unhappy_church_strong }
				random = { chance = 30 remove_country_modifier = unhappy_church_strong }
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = { has_country_modifier = unhappy_church_powerful }
				random = { chance = 20 remove_country_modifier = unhappy_church_powerful }
			}
		}
	}
	
	
	option = {
		name = dg_orthodox.026.a #Choose the most educated bishop #Theologian > Zealous > Controversial > Obedient
		ai_chance = { factor = 40 }
		owner = {
			if = {
				limit = { ADM = 6 }
				random_list = {
					10 = { set_country_flag = patriarch_zealous custom_tooltip = patriarch_zealous }
					90 = { set_country_flag = patriarch_theologian custom_tooltip = patriarch_theologian }
				}
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = { ADM = 5 }
				random_list = {
					20 = { set_country_flag = patriarch_zealous custom_tooltip = patriarch_zealous }
					80 = { set_country_flag = patriarch_theologian custom_tooltip = patriarch_theologian }
				}
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = { ADM = 4 }
				random_list = {
					40 = { set_country_flag = patriarch_zealous custom_tooltip = patriarch_zealous }
					70 = { set_country_flag = patriarch_theologian custom_tooltip = patriarch_theologian }
				}
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = { ADM = 3 }
				random_list = {
					10 = { set_country_flag = patriarch_controversial custom_tooltip = patriarch_controversial }
					40 = { set_country_flag = patriarch_zealous custom_tooltip = patriarch_zealous }
					60 = { set_country_flag = patriarch_theologian custom_tooltip = patriarch_theologian }
				}
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = { ADM = 2 }
				random_list = {
					10 = { set_country_flag = patriarch_obedient custom_tooltip = patriarch_obedient }
					15 = { set_country_flag = patriarch_corrupt custom_tooltip = patriarch_corrupt }
					35 = { set_country_flag = patriarch_controversial custom_tooltip = patriarch_controversial }
					50 = { set_country_flag = patriarch_theologian custom_tooltip = patriarch_theologian }
				}
			}
			else = {
				random_list = {
					10 = { set_country_flag = patriarch_obedient custom_tooltip = patriarch_obedient }
					20 = { set_country_flag = patriarch_controversial custom_tooltip = patriarch_controversial }
					40 = { set_country_flag = patriarch_corrupt custom_tooltip = patriarch_corrupt }
					40 = { set_country_flag = patriarch_theologian custom_tooltip = patriarch_theologian }
				}
			}
			hidden_effect = { set_variable = { which = patriarch_hostility value = 0 } }
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				NOT = { is_core = owner }
				has_owner_culture = no
				has_owner_accepted_culture = no
			}
			random = {
				chance = 50
				owner = {
					set_country_flag = patriarch_hostile
					clr_country_flag = patriarch_obedient
					clr_country_flag = patriarch_controversial
					clr_country_flag = patriarch_theologian
					clr_country_flag = patriarch_zealous
					clr_country_flag = patriarch_corrupt
				}
			}
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = dg_orthodox.026.b #Choose the most pliant bishop #Obedient > Zealous > Theologian > Controversial
		ai_chance = { factor = 40 }
		owner = {
			if = {
				limit = { ADM = 6 }
				random_list = {
					10 = { set_country_flag = patriarch_zealous custom_tooltip = patriarch_zealous }
					90 = { set_country_flag = patriarch_obedient custom_tooltip = patriarch_obedient }
				}
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = { ADM = 5 }
				random_list = {
					20 = { set_country_flag = patriarch_zealous custom_tooltip = patriarch_zealous }
					80 = { set_country_flag = patriarch_obedient custom_tooltip = patriarch_obedient }
				}
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = { ADM = 4 }
				random_list = {
					40 = { set_country_flag = patriarch_zealous custom_tooltip = patriarch_zealous }
					70 = { set_country_flag = patriarch_obedient custom_tooltip = patriarch_obedient }
				}
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = { ADM = 3 }
				random_list = {
					10 = { set_country_flag = patriarch_theologian custom_tooltip = patriarch_theologian }
					40 = { set_country_flag = patriarch_zealous custom_tooltip = patriarch_zealous }
					60 = { set_country_flag = patriarch_obedient custom_tooltip = patriarch_obedient }
				}
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = { ADM = 2 }
				random_list = {
					10 = { set_country_flag = patriarch_controversial custom_tooltip = patriarch_controversial }
					15 = { set_country_flag = patriarch_corrupt custom_tooltip = patriarch_corrupt }
					35 = { set_country_flag = patriarch_theologian custom_tooltip = patriarch_theologian }
					50 = { set_country_flag = patriarch_obedient custom_tooltip = patriarch_obedient }
				}
			}
			else = {
				random_list = {
					10 = { set_country_flag = patriarch_controversial custom_tooltip = patriarch_controversial }
					20 = { set_country_flag = patriarch_theologian custom_tooltip = patriarch_theologian }
					40 = { set_country_flag = patriarch_corrupt custom_tooltip = patriarch_corrupt }
					40 = { set_country_flag = patriarch_obedient custom_tooltip = patriarch_obedient }
				}
			}
			hidden_effect = { set_variable = { which = patriarch_hostility value = 0 } }
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				NOT = { is_core = owner }
				has_owner_culture = no
				has_owner_accepted_culture = no
			}
			random = {
				chance = 50
				owner = {
					set_country_flag = patriarch_hostile
					clr_country_flag = patriarch_obedient
					clr_country_flag = patriarch_controversial
					clr_country_flag = patriarch_theologian
					clr_country_flag = patriarch_zealous
					clr_country_flag = patriarch_corrupt
				}
			}
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = dg_orthodox.026.c #Choose the most pious bishop #Zealous > Theologian > Controversial > Obedient
		ai_chance = { factor = 40 }
		owner = {
			if = {
				limit = { ADM = 6 }
				random_list = {
					10 = { set_country_flag = patriarch_theologian custom_tooltip = patriarch_theologian }
					90 = { set_country_flag = patriarch_zealous custom_tooltip = patriarch_zealous }
				}
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = { ADM = 5 }
				random_list = {
					20 = { set_country_flag = patriarch_theologian custom_tooltip = patriarch_theologian }
					80 = { set_country_flag = patriarch_zealous custom_tooltip = patriarch_zealous }
				}
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = { ADM = 4 }
				random_list = {
					40 = { set_country_flag = patriarch_theologian custom_tooltip = patriarch_theologian }
					70 = { set_country_flag = patriarch_zealous custom_tooltip = patriarch_zealous }
				}
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = { ADM = 3 }
				random_list = {
					10 = { set_country_flag = patriarch_controversial custom_tooltip = patriarch_controversial }
					40 = { set_country_flag = patriarch_theologian custom_tooltip = patriarch_theologian }
					60 = { set_country_flag = patriarch_zealous custom_tooltip = patriarch_zealous }
				}
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = { ADM = 2 }
				random_list = {
					20 = { set_country_flag = patriarch_controversial custom_tooltip = patriarch_controversial }
					40 = { set_country_flag = patriarch_theologian custom_tooltip = patriarch_theologian }
					50 = { set_country_flag = patriarch_zealous custom_tooltip = patriarch_zealous }
				}
			}
			else = {
				random_list = {
					10 = { set_country_flag = patriarch_obedient custom_tooltip = patriarch_obedient }
					20 = { set_country_flag = patriarch_controversial custom_tooltip = patriarch_controversial }
					40 = { set_country_flag = patriarch_theologian custom_tooltip = patriarch_theologian }
					40 = { set_country_flag = patriarch_zealous custom_tooltip = patriarch_zealous }
				}
			}
			hidden_effect = { set_variable = { which = patriarch_hostility value = 0 } }
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				NOT = { is_core = owner }
				has_owner_culture = no
				has_owner_accepted_culture = no
			}
			random = {
				chance = 50
				owner = {
					set_country_flag = patriarch_hostile
					clr_country_flag = patriarch_obedient
					clr_country_flag = patriarch_controversial
					clr_country_flag = patriarch_theologian
					clr_country_flag = patriarch_zealous
					clr_country_flag = patriarch_corrupt
				}
			}
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = dg_orthodox.026.e #Leave the position vacant
		trigger = {
			owner = {
				NOT = { has_country_flag = independent_patriarchate }
				OR = {
					has_country_flag = patriarch_controversial
					has_country_flag = patriarch_hostile
					has_country_flag = veliki_gosudar
					NOT = { piety = -0.20 }
				}
			}
		}
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 10
			modifier = {
				owner = { check_variable = { which = patriarch_hostility value = 1 } }
				factor = 2
			}
			modifier = {
				owner = { check_variable = { which = patriarch_hostility value = 2 } }
				factor = 2
			}
			modifier = {
				owner = { has_country_flag = veliki_gosudar }
				factor = 2
			}
			modifier = {
				owner = { NOT = { piety = -0.20 } }
				factor = 2
			}
			modifier = {
				owner = { NOT = { piety = -0.60 } }
				factor = 2
			}
		}
		owner = {
			set_country_flag = patriarchate_vacant
			if = {
				limit = { patriarch_authority = 0.80 }
				add_country_modifier = { name = unhappy_church_powerful duration = 2000 }
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = { patriarch_authority = 0.60 }
				add_country_modifier = { name = unhappy_church_strong duration = 2000 }
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = { patriarch_authority = 0.40 }
				add_country_modifier = { name = unhappy_church_moderate duration = 2000 }
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = { patriarch_authority = 0.20 }
				add_country_modifier = { name = unhappy_church_weak duration = 2000 }
			}
			else = {
				add_country_modifier = { name = unhappy_church_impotent duration = 2000 }
			}
			add_patriarch_authority = -0.10
			hidden_effect = { set_variable = { which = patriarch_hostility value = 0 } }
		}
	}
	after = {
		owner = { dg_patriarch_triggers = yes }
	}
}

country_event = { #38 - A New Patriarch
	
	id = dg_miaphysite.038
	title = dg_miaphysite.038.t
	desc = dg_miaphysite.038.d
	picture = orthodox_basilica
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	option = {
		name = dg_miaphysite.038.a #Send tribute to him
		trigger = {
			OR = {
				is_free_or_tributary_trigger = yes
				FROM = { owner = { overlord_of = ROOT } }
				overlord = { NOT = { religion = coptic } }
			}
		}
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 35
			modifier = {
				any_owned_province = { has_province_modifier = coptic_patriarchate }
				religion = coptic
				factor = 0
			}
			modifier = {
				FROM = { owner = { overlord_of = ROOT } }
				NOT = { liberty_desire = 35 }
				factor = 2
			}
			modifier = {
				FROM = { owner = { overlord_of = ROOT } }
				NOT = { liberty_desire = 50 }
				factor = 2
			}
			modifier = {
				FROM = { owner = { overlord_of = ROOT } }
				NOT = { liberty_desire = 75 }
				factor = 2
			}
			modifier = {
				NOT = { FROM = { owner = { religion = ROOT } } }
				factor = 0
			}
		}
		reverse_add_opinion = { who = FROM modifier = recognized_patriarch_authority }
		if = {
			limit = { piety = 0.60 }
			add_prestige = -2
		}
		else_if = {

			add_prestige = -4
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = { piety = -0.20 }
			add_prestige = -6
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = { piety = -0.60 }
			add_prestige = -8
		}
		else = {
			add_prestige = -10
		}
		set_country_flag = send_tribute_to_patriarch
		FROM = { province_event = { id = dg_miaphysite.039 days = 40 } }
	}
	option = {
		name = dg_miaphysite.038.b #Send congratulations to him
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 50
			modifier = {
				FROM = { owner = { primary_culture = ROOT } }
				factor = 2
			}
		}
		reverse_add_opinion = { who = FROM modifier = obeyed_religious_leader }
		FROM = { province_event = { id = dg_miaphysite.039 days = 40 } }
	}
	option = {
		name = dg_miaphysite.038.c #Declare him illegitimate
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 35
			modifier = {
				FROM = { owner = { NOT = { religion = ROOT } } }
				factor = 2
			}
			modifier = {
				FROM = { owner = { is_rival = ROOT } }
				factor = 2
			}
			modifier = {
				FROM = { owner = { is_enemy = ROOT } }
				factor = 2
			}
			modifier = {
				FROM = { owner = { war_with = ROOT } }
				factor = 2
			}
			modifier = {
				FROM = { owner = { truce_with = ROOT } }
				factor = 2
			}
			modifier = {
				FROM = { owner = { marriage_with = ROOT } }
				factor = 0.5
			}
			modifier = {
				FROM = { owner = { alliance_with = ROOT } }
				factor = 0.5
			}
		}
		trigger = { NOT = { FROM = { owner = { overlord_of = ROOT } } } }
		reverse_add_opinion = { who = FROM modifier = disobeyed_religious_leader }
		FROM = { province_event = { id = dg_miaphysite.040 days = 40 } }
	}
}

					add_prestige = 8
				}
				else_if = {
					limit = { FROM = { total_development = 15 } }
					add_prestige = 6
				}
				else_if = {
					limit = { FROM = { total_development = 10 } }
					add_prestige = 4
				}
				else = {
					add_prestige = 2
				}
				FROM = { clr_country_flag = send_tribute_to_patriarch }
			}
			else = {
				reverse_add_opinion = { who = FROM modifier = obeyed_religious_leader }
				if = {
					limit = { FROM = { total_development = 60 } }
					add_prestige = 5
				}
				else_if = {
					limit = { FROM = { total_development = 35 } }
					add_prestige = 4
				}
				else_if = {
					limit = { FROM = { total_development = 15 } }
					add_prestige = 3
				}
				else_if = {
					limit = { FROM = { total_development = 10 } }
					add_prestige = 2
				}
				else = {
					add_prestige = 1
				}
			}
		}
	}
}
