country_event = { #41 - Patriarch protests the treatment of his people
	
	id = dg_miaphysite.041
	title = dg_miaphysite.041.t
	desc = dg_miaphysite.041.d
	picture = orthodox_metropolitan
	
	trigger = {
		any_owned_province = { has_province_modifier = coptic_patriarchate_captive }
		OR = {
			has_country_flag = religious_turmoil_coptic
			any_owned_province = {
				has_missionary = yes
				religion = coptic
				NOT = { has_province_modifier = missionary_failure }
			}
		}
		NOT = { has_country_modifier = coptic_patriarch_timer }
		NOT = { has_disaster = religious_civil_war }
	}
	
	mean_time_to_happen = { months = 6 }
	
	immediate = {
		hidden_effect = {
			random_owned_province = {
				limit = { has_province_modifier = coptic_patriarchate_captive }
				set_province_flag = patriarch_protest
				every_province = {
					limit = { region = PREV }
					if = {
						limit = { check_variable = { which = coptic value = 10 } }
						PREV = { change_variable = { which = patriarch_influence value = 5 } }
					}
					else_if = {
						limit = { check_variable = { which = coptic value = 8 } }
						PREV = { change_variable = { which = patriarch_influence value = 4 } }
					}
					else_if = {
						limit = { check_variable = { which = coptic value = 6 } }
						PREV = { change_variable = { which = patriarch_influence value = 3 } }
					}
					else_if = {
						limit = { check_variable = { which = coptic value = 4 } }
						PREV = { change_variable = { which = patriarch_influence value = 2 } }
					}
					else_if = {
						limit = { check_variable = { which = coptic value = 2 } }
						PREV = { change_variable = { which = patriarch_influence value = 1 } }
					}
				}
			}
		}
	}
	
	option = {
		name = dg_miaphysite.041.a #Back down
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 30
			modifier = {
				has_country_flag = christians_tolerated
				factor = 2
			}
			modifier = {
				has_country_flag = christians_permitted
				factor = 1.4
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = { piety = 0.60 }
			add_prestige = -10
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = { piety = 0.20 }
			add_prestige = -8
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = { piety = -0.20 }
			add_prestige = -6
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = { piety = -0.60 }
			add_prestige = -4
		}
		else = {
			add_prestige = -2
		}
		clr_country_flag = religious_turmoil_coptic
		if = {
			limit = { NOT = { has_country_modifier = religious_intolerance } NOT = { has_country_modifier = religious_tolerance } }
			add_country_modifier = { name = religious_tolerance duration = 1000 }
			add_piety = -0.20
		}
		if = {
			limit = { has_country_modifier = religious_intolerance }
			remove_country_modifier = religious_intolerance
			add_piety = -0.20
		}
		if = {
			limit = { any_owned_province = { religion = coptic has_missionary = yes } }
			every_owned_province = {
				limit = { religion = coptic has_missionary = yes }
				add_province_modifier = { name = missionary_failure duration = 3000 }
			}
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			random_owned_province = {
				limit = { has_province_flag = patriarch_protest }
				clr_province_flag = patriarch_protest
				set_variable = { which = patriarch_influence value = 0 }
			}
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = dg_miaphysite.041.b #Replace him with a more pliant man
		ai_chance = { factor = 40 }
		add_adm_power = -5
		custom_tooltip = puppet_catholicos_explained
		add_country_modifier = { name = coptic_patriarch_timer duration = 3000 hidden = yes }
		random = {
			chance = 30
			random_owned_province = {
				limit = { has_province_flag = patriarch_protest }
				remove_province_modifier = coptic_patriarchate_captive
				add_permanent_province_modifier = { name = coptic_patriarchate_vacant duration = -1 }
			}
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			random_owned_province = {
				limit = { has_province_flag = patriarch_protest }
				clr_province_flag = patriarch_protest
				set_variable = { which = patriarch_influence value = 0 }
			}
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = dg_miaphysite.041.c #Shut down the Patriarchate
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 30
			modifier = {
				has_country_flag = christians_permitted
				factor = 0.5
			}
		}
		trigger = { NOT = { has_country_flag = christians_tolerated } }
		random_owned_province = {
			limit = { has_province_flag = patriarch_protest }
			remove_province_modifier = coptic_patriarchate_captive
			if = {
				limit = { check_variable = { which = patriarch_influence value = 25 } }
				owner = { add_treasury = 250 }
				add_nationalism = 10
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = { check_variable = { which = patriarch_influence value = 16 } }
				owner = { add_treasury = 200 }
				add_nationalism = 8
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = { check_variable = { which = patriarch_influence value = 9 } }
				owner = { add_treasury = 150 }
				add_nationalism = 6
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = { check_variable = { which = patriarch_influence value = 4 } }
				owner = { add_treasury = 100 }
				add_nationalism = 4
			}
			else = {
				owner = { add_treasury = 50 }
				add_nationalism = 2
			}
			add_permanent_province_modifier = { name = coptic_patriarchate_vacant duration = -1 }
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			random_owned_province = {
				limit = { has_province_flag = patriarch_protest }
				clr_province_flag = patriarch_protest
				set_variable = { which = patriarch_influence value = 0 }
			}
		}
	}
}

		remove_province_modifier = coptic_pentarchy

province_event = { #45 - The Catholicos returns home
	
	id = dg_miaphysite.045
	title = dg_miaphysite.045.t
	desc = dg_miaphysite.045.d
	picture = orthodox_patriarch_migration
	
	trigger = {
		OR = {
			AND = {
				has_province_flag = miaphysite_catholicate_of_antioch
				NOT = { has_province_flag = miaphysite_catholicos_of_antioch }
			}
			AND = {
				has_province_flag = miaphysite_catholicate_of_alexandria
				NOT = { has_province_flag = miaphysite_catholicos_of_alexandria }
			}
			AND = {
				has_province_flag = miaphysite_catholicate_of_jerusalem
				NOT = { has_province_flag = miaphysite_catholicos_of_jerusalem }
			}
		}
		owner = { religion = coptic }
		has_siege = no
		controlled_by = owner
	}
	
	mean_time_to_happen = { months = 6 }
	
	option = {
		name = dg_miaphysite.045.a #Welcome home
		owner = {
			if = {
				limit = { piety = 0.60 }
				add_prestige = 16
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = { piety = 0.20 }
				add_prestige = 12
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = { piety = -0.20 }
				add_prestige = 8
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = { piety = -0.60 }
				add_prestige = 4
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = { has_province_flag = miaphysite_catholicate_of_antioch }
			if = {
				limit = {
					antioch_patriarch_area = {
						has_province_flag = miaphysite_catholicos_of_antioch
						owned_by = ROOT
					}
				}
				antioch_patriarch_area = {
					limit = {
						has_province_flag = miaphysite_catholicos_of_antioch
					}
					clr_province_flag = miaphysite_catholicos_of_antioch
					clr_province_flag = coptic_pentarchy
					clr_province_flag = coptic_patriarchate
					remove_province_modifier = coptic_patriarchate
					remove_province_modifier = coptic_pentarchy
					remove_province_modifier = coptic_patriarchate_captive
					remove_province_modifier = coptic_patriarchate_vacant
					remove_province_modifier = coptic_archbishopric
				}
			}
			else = {
				antioch_patriarch_area = {
					limit = {
						has_province_flag = miaphysite_catholicos_of_antioch
					}
					province_event = { id = dg_miaphysite.044 }
				}
			}
			hidden_effect = { set_province_flag = miaphysite_catholicos_of_antioch }
		}
		if = {
			limit = { has_province_flag = miaphysite_catholicate_of_alexandria }
			if = {
				limit = {
					alexandria_patriarch_area = {
						has_province_flag = miaphysite_catholicos_of_alexandria
						owned_by = ROOT
					}
				}
				alexandria_patriarch_area = {
					limit = {
						has_province_flag = miaphysite_catholicos_of_alexandria
					}
					clr_province_flag = miaphysite_catholicos_of_alexandria
					clr_province_flag = coptic_pentarchy
					clr_province_flag = coptic_patriarchate
					remove_province_modifier = coptic_patriarchate
					remove_province_modifier = coptic_pentarchy
					remove_province_modifier = coptic_patriarchate_captive
					remove_province_modifier = coptic_patriarchate_vacant
					remove_province_modifier = coptic_archbishopric
				}
			}
			else = {
				alexandria_patriarch_area = {
					limit = {
						has_province_flag = miaphysite_catholicos_of_alexandria
					}
					province_event = { id = dg_miaphysite.044 }
				}
			}
			hidden_effect = { set_province_flag = miaphysite_catholicos_of_alexandria }
		}
		if = {
			limit = { has_province_flag = miaphysite_catholicate_of_jerusalem }
			if = {
				limit = {
					jerusalem_patriarch_area = {
						has_province_flag = miaphysite_catholicos_of_jerusalem
						owned_by = ROOT
					}
				}
				jerusalem_patriarch_area = {
					limit = {
						has_province_flag = miaphysite_catholicos_of_jerusalem
					}
					clr_province_flag = miaphysite_catholicos_of_jerusalem
					clr_province_flag = coptic_pentarchy
					clr_province_flag = coptic_patriarchate
					remove_province_modifier = coptic_patriarchate
					remove_province_modifier = coptic_pentarchy
					remove_province_modifier = coptic_patriarchate_captive
					remove_province_modifier = coptic_patriarchate_vacant
					remove_province_modifier = coptic_archbishopric
				}
			}
			else = {

					limit = {
						has_province_flag = miaphysite_catholicos_of_jerusalem
					}
					province_event = { id = dg_miaphysite.044 }
				}
			}
			hidden_effect = { set_province_flag = miaphysite_catholicos_of_jerusalem }
		}
		if = {
			limit = { NOT = { check_variable = { which = coptic value = 21 } } }
			custom_tooltip = convert_20
			hidden_effect = { change_variable = { which = converted_heathens value = 4 } }
		}
		set_province_flag = coptic_pentarchy
		set_province_flag = coptic_patriarchate
	}
}

province_event = { #46 - Election of the Catholicos (simony involved)
	
	id = dg_miaphysite.046
	title = dg_miaphysite.046.t
	desc = dg_miaphysite.046.d
	picture = miaphysite_monks_argument_saffron
	
	trigger = {
		has_province_modifier = coptic_patriarchate_captive
		NOT = { has_province_modifier = greedy_bishop }
		NOT = { owner = { has_country_flag = religious_turmoil_coptic } }
	}
	
	mean_time_to_happen = { years = 41 }
	
	immediate = {
		if = {
			limit = { owner = { NOT = { religion_group = christian } } }
			custom_tooltip = dg_miaphysite.046.d_heathen
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			every_province = {
				limit = { region = ROOT }
				if = {
					limit = { check_variable = { which = coptic value = 10 } }
					PREV = { change_variable = { which = patriarch_influence value = 5 } }
				}
				else_if = {
					limit = { check_variable = { which = coptic value = 8 } }
					PREV = { change_variable = { which = patriarch_influence value = 4 } }
				}
				else_if = {
					limit = { check_variable = { which = coptic value = 6 } }
					PREV = { change_variable = { which = patriarch_influence value = 3 } }
				}
				else_if = {
					limit = { check_variable = { which = coptic value = 4 } }
					PREV = { change_variable = { which = patriarch_influence value = 2 } }
				}
				else_if = {
					limit = { check_variable = { which = coptic value = 2 } }
					PREV = { change_variable = { which = patriarch_influence value = 1 } }
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					any_province = {
						region = ROOT
						NOT = { province_id = ROOT }
						OR = {
							has_province_modifier = coptic_patriarchate
							has_province_modifier = coptic_archbishopric
							has_province_modifier = coptic_patriarchate_captive
						}
					}
				}
				multiply_variable = { which = patriarch_influence value = 0.7 }
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					any_province = {
						region = ROOT
						NOT = { province_id = ROOT }
						has_province_flag = coptic_pentarchy
					}
				}
				multiply_variable = { which = patriarch_influence value = 0.7 }
			}
		}
	}
	
	option = {
		name = dg_miaphysite.046.a #Award the seat to the highest bidder
		ai_chance = { factor = 50 }
		add_province_modifier = { name = greedy_bishop duration = 2000 }
		if = {
			limit = { check_variable = { which = patriarch_influence value = 24 } }
			owner = { add_treasury = 18 }
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = { check_variable = { which = patriarch_influence value = 18 } }
			owner = { add_treasury = 12 }
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = { check_variable = { which = patriarch_influence value = 12 } }
			owner = { add_treasury = 8 }
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = { check_variable = { which = patriarch_influence value = 6 } }
			owner = { add_treasury = 4 }
		}
		else = {
			owner = { add_treasury = 2 }
		}
		hidden_effect = { set_variable = { which = patriarch_influence value = 0 } }
	}
	option = {
		name = dg_miaphysite.046.b #Try to choose the better man
		ai_chance = { factor = 25 }
		trigger = {
			owner = {
				OR = {
					religion_group = christian
					coptic = 1
				}
			}
		}
		add_nationalism = -3
		hidden_effect = { set_variable = { which = patriarch_influence value = 0 } }
	}
	option = {
		name = dg_miaphysite.046.c #Get the noose ready!
		ai_chance = { factor = 25 }
		trigger = { NOT = { owner = { religion_group = christian } } }
		add_province_modifier = { name = religious_scandal_province duration = 1000 }
		add_province_modifier = { name = greedy_bishop duration = 3000 }
		if = {
			limit = { check_variable = { which = patriarch_influence value = 24 } }
			owner = { add_treasury = 24 }
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = { check_variable = { which = patriarch_influence value = 18 } }
			owner = { add_treasury = 18 }
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = { check_variable = { which = patriarch_influence value = 12 } }
			owner = { add_treasury = 12 }
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = { check_variable = { which = patriarch_influence value = 6 } }
			owner = { add_treasury = 6 }
		}
		else = {
			owner = { add_treasury = 3 }
		}
		owner = {
			every_owned_province = {
				limit = {
					OR = {
						religion = coptic
						province_id = ROOT
					}
					region = ROOT
				}
				hidden_effect = {
					set_variable = { which = added_unrest value = 3 }
					add_base_unrest = yes
				}
				custom_tooltip = added_unrest_3
			}
		}
		hidden_effect = { set_variable = { which = patriarch_influence value = 0 } }
	}
}

country_event = { #47 - Vacant Office
	
	id = dg_miaphysite.047
	title = dg_miaphysite.047.t
	desc = dg_miaphysite.047.d
	picture = miaphysite_monastery_saffron
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	trigger = {
		NOT = { has_country_flag = patriarch_controversial }
		NOT = { has_country_flag = patriarch_hostile }
		NOT = { has_country_flag = patriarch_obedient }
		NOT = { has_country_flag = patriarch_zealous }
		NOT = { has_country_flag = patriarch_theologian }
		NOT = { has_country_flag = patriarch_corrupt }
	}
	
	immediate = {
		if = {
			limit = { NOT = { has_country_flag = bribe_for_catholicos } }
			custom_tooltip = dg_miaphysite.047.d_bribe
		}
	}
	
	option = {
		name = dg_miaphysite.047.a #Send the [From.Monarch.GetName] a request
		trigger = { NOT = { has_country_flag = request_for_catholicos } }
		ai_chance = { factor = 40 }
		if = {
			limit = { capital_scope = { continent = europe } }
			antioch_patriarch_area = {
				limit = {
					has_province_flag = miaphysite_catholicos_of_antioch
				}
				owner = { country_event = { id = dg_miaphysite.048 days = 60 } }
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = { capital_scope = { NOT = { continent = europe } } }
			alexandria_patriarch_area = {
				limit = {
					has_province_flag = miaphysite_catholicos_of_alexandria
				}
				owner = { country_event = { id = dg_miaphysite.048 days = 60 } }
			}
		}
		set_country_flag = request_for_catholicos
	}
	option = {
		name = dg_miaphysite.047.b #Send the [From.Monarch.GetName] a bribe
		trigger = { NOT = { has_country_flag = bribe_for_catholicos } }
		ai_chance = { factor = 40 }
		if = {
			limit = { capital_scope = { continent = europe } }
			antioch_patriarch_area = {
				limit = {
					has_province_flag = miaphysite_catholicos_of_antioch
				}
				owner = { country_event = { id = dg_miaphysite.048 days = 60 } }
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = { capital_scope = { NOT = { continent = europe } } }
			alexandria_patriarch_area = {
				limit = {
					has_province_flag = miaphysite_catholicos_of_alexandria
				}
				owner = { country_event = { id = dg_miaphysite.048 days = 60 } }
			}
		}
		set_country_flag = request_for_catholicos
		set_country_flag = bribe_for_catholicos
		if = {
			limit = { monthly_income = 50 }
			add_treasury = -50
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = { monthly_income = 25 }
			add_treasury = -25
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = { monthly_income = 10 }
			add_treasury = -10
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = { monthly_income = 5 }
			add_treasury = -5
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = { monthly_income = 2 }
			add_treasury = -2
		}
		else = {
			add_treasury = -1
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = dg_miaphysite.047.c #Leave the position vacant for now
		ai_chance = { factor = 20 }
		if = {
			limit = { piety = 0.60 }
			add_prestige = -4
			add_legitimacy = -4
			add_republican_tradition = -2
			add_devotion = -8
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = { piety = 0.20 }
			add_prestige = -3
			add_legitimacy = -3
			add_republican_tradition = -1.5
			add_devotion = -6
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = { piety = -0.20 }
			add_prestige = -2
			add_legitimacy = -2
			add_republican_tradition = -1
			add_devotion = -4
		}
		else = {
			add_prestige = -1
			add_legitimacy = -1
			add_republican_tradition = -0.5
			add_devotion = -2
		}
	}
}

	}

				factor = 1.4
			}
			modifier = {
				FROM = { num_of_cities = ROOT }
				factor = 1.4
			}
			modifier = {
				FROM = { army_size = ROOT }
				factor = 1.4
			}
			modifier = {
				FROM = { war_with = ROOT }
				factor = 0
			}
			modifier = {
				is_rival = FROM
				factor = 0.7
			}
			modifier = {

				factor = 0.7
			}
			modifier = {

				factor = 1.4
			}
			modifier = {

		}
		else = {
			reverse_add_opinion = { who = FROM modifier = aided_coreligionists_decadent }
		}
		if = {
			limit = { FROM = { has_country_flag = bribe_for_catholicos } }
			if = {
				limit = { FROM = { monthly_income = 50 } }
				add_treasury = 50
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = { FROM = { monthly_income = 25 } }
				add_treasury = 25
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = { FROM = { monthly_income = 10 } }
				add_treasury = 10
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = { FROM = { monthly_income = 5 } }
				add_treasury = 5
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = { FROM = { monthly_income = 2 } }
				add_treasury = 2
			}
			else = {
				add_treasury = 1
			}
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = dg_miaphysite.048.b #Forbid him from going
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 60
			modifier = {
				FROM = { overlord_of = ROOT }
				factor = 0
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = { FROM = { piety = 0.60 } }
			reverse_add_opinion = { who = FROM modifier = mistreated_coreligionists_fanatical }
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = { FROM = { piety = 0.20 } }
			reverse_add_opinion = { who = FROM modifier = mistreated_coreligionists_pious }
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = { FROM = { piety = -0.20 } }
			reverse_add_opinion = { who = FROM modifier = mistreated_coreligionists_observant }
		}
		else = {
			reverse_add_opinion = { who = FROM modifier = mistreated_coreligionists_decadent }
		}
		FROM = { country_event = { id = dg_miaphysite.047 days = 60 } }
	}
}

country_event = { #49 - Arrival of the Metropolitan
	
	id = dg_miaphysite.049
	title = dg_miaphysite.049.t
	desc = dg_miaphysite.049.d
	picture = miaphysite_pilgrims_return_saffron
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	option = {
		name = dg_orthodox.025.b #Receive the new metropolitan
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_country_modifier = foreign_liturgy
				has_country_modifier = heretic_liturgy
			}
			random_list = {
				20 = { set_country_flag = patriarch_zealous custom_tooltip = patriarch_zealous }
				25 = { set_country_flag = patriarch_theologian custom_tooltip = patriarch_theologian }
				30 = { set_country_flag = patriarch_controversial custom_tooltip = patriarch_controversial }
				25 = { set_country_flag = patriarch_hostile custom_tooltip = patriarch_hostile }
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					has_country_modifier = foreign_liturgy
					has_country_modifier = heretic_liturgy
				}
				NOT = {
					AND = {
						has_country_modifier = foreign_liturgy
						has_country_modifier = heretic_liturgy
					}
				}
			}
			random_list = {
				5 = { set_country_flag = patriarch_obedient custom_tooltip = patriarch_obedient }
				25 = { set_country_flag = patriarch_zealous custom_tooltip = patriarch_zealous }
				25 = { set_country_flag = patriarch_theologian custom_tooltip = patriarch_theologian }
				25 = { set_country_flag = patriarch_controversial custom_tooltip = patriarch_controversial }
				15 = { set_country_flag = patriarch_hostile custom_tooltip = patriarch_hostile }
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				NOT = { has_country_modifier = foreign_liturgy }
				NOT = { has_country_modifier = heretic_liturgy }
			}
			random_list = {
				25 = { set_country_flag = patriarch_obedient custom_tooltip = patriarch_obedient }
				25 = { set_country_flag = patriarch_zealous custom_tooltip = patriarch_zealous }
				25 = { set_country_flag = patriarch_theologian custom_tooltip = patriarch_theologian }
				20 = { set_country_flag = patriarch_controversial custom_tooltip = patriarch_controversial }
				5 = { set_country_flag = patriarch_hostile custom_tooltip = patriarch_hostile }
			}
		}
	}
}

								desert_trigger = yes
							}
							NOT = { has_province_modifier = monastery_stephanite }

							limit = {
								region = PREV

									if = {
										limit = { has_country_flag = monastery_sonsofgrace }
										every_owned_province = {
											limit = { has_province_flag = event_target }
											add_province_modifier = { name = monastery_sonsofgrace duration = 10000 }
										}
									}
									if = {
										limit = { has_country_flag = monastery_zakristos }
										every_owned_province = {
											limit = { has_province_flag = event_target }
											add_province_modifier = { name = monastery_zakristos duration = 10000 }
										}
									}
									if = {
										limit = { has_country_flag = monastery_stephanite }
										every_owned_province = {
											limit = { has_province_flag = event_target }
											add_province_modifier = { name = monastery_stephanite duration = 10000 }
										}
									}
									every_owned_province = { clr_province_flag = event_target }
								}
							}
						}
					}
				}
				12 = { #Theological Conflicts
					if = {
						limit = {
							is_at_war = no
							NOT = { has_country_modifier = religious_controversy }
						}
						#Sabbath Controversy (15th century)
						if = {
							limit = {
								NOT = { has_country_flag = miaphysite_controversy }
								NOT = { has_country_flag = miaphysite_controversy_sabbath_resolved }
								any_owned_province = { has_province_modifier = monastery_unctionist }
								OR = {
									NOT = { has_country_flag = miaphysite_doctrine_unctionist }
									any_owned_province = { has_province_modifier = monastery_unity }
									any_owned_province = { has_province_modifier = monastery_zakristos }
									any_owned_province = { has_province_modifier = monastery_stephanite }
									any_owned_province = { has_province_modifier = monastery_sonsofgrace }
								}
							}
							set_country_flag = miaphysite_controversy
							set_country_flag = miaphysite_controversy_sabbath
						}
						if = {
							limit = {
								NOT = { has_country_flag = miaphysite_controversy }
								NOT = { has_country_flag = miaphysite_controversy_sabbath_resolved }
								any_owned_province = { has_province_modifier = monastery_zakristos }
								OR = {
									NOT = { has_country_flag = miaphysite_doctrine_unctionist }
									any_owned_province = { has_province_modifier = monastery_unity }
									any_owned_province = { has_province_modifier = monastery_unctionist }
									any_owned_province = { has_province_modifier = monastery_stephanite }
									any_owned_province = { has_province_modifier = monastery_sonsofgrace }
								}
							}
							set_country_flag = miaphysite_controversy
							set_country_flag = miaphysite_controversy_sabbath
						}
						#Icons (ahistorical 16th century)
						if = {
							limit = {
								NOT = { has_country_flag = miaphysite_controversy }
								NOT = { has_country_flag = miaphysite_controversy_icons_resolved }
								any_owned_province = { has_province_modifier = monastery_stephanite }
								OR = {
									NOT = { has_country_flag = miaphysite_doctrine_stephanite }
									any_owned_province = { has_province_modifier = monastery_unity }
									any_owned_province = { has_province_modifier = monastery_zakristos }
									any_owned_province = { has_province_modifier = monastery_unctionist }
									any_owned_province = { has_province_modifier = monastery_sonsofgrace }
								}
							}
							set_country_flag = miaphysite_controversy
							set_country_flag = miaphysite_controversy_icons
						}
						#Christology (17th century)
						if = {
							limit = {
								has_country_flag = met_other_christians
								NOT = { has_country_flag = miaphysite_controversy_christology_resolved }
							}
							if = {
								limit = {
									NOT = { has_country_flag = miaphysite_controversy }
									any_owned_province = { has_province_modifier = monastery_unctionist }
									OR = {
										NOT = { has_country_flag = miaphysite_doctrine_unctionist }
										any_owned_province = { has_province_modifier = monastery_unity }
										any_owned_province = { has_province_modifier = monastery_zakristos }
										any_owned_province = { has_province_modifier = monastery_sonsofgrace }
										any_owned_province = { has_province_modifier = monastery_stephanite }
									}
								}
								set_country_flag = miaphysite_controversy
								set_country_flag = miaphysite_controversy_christology
							}
							if = {
								limit = {
									NOT = { has_country_flag = miaphysite_controversy }
									any_owned_province = { has_province_modifier = monastery_sonsofgrace }
									OR = {
										NOT = { has_country_flag = miaphysite_doctrine_sonsofgrace }
										any_owned_province = { has_province_modifier = monastery_unity }
										any_owned_province = { has_province_modifier = monastery_zakristos }
										any_owned_province = { has_province_modifier = monastery_unctionist }
										any_owned_province = { has_province_modifier = monastery_stephanite }
									}
								}
								set_country_flag = miaphysite_controversy
								set_country_flag = miaphysite_controversy_christology
							}
							if = {
								limit = {
									NOT = { has_country_flag = miaphysite_controversy }
									any_owned_province = { has_province_modifier = monastery_zakristos }
									OR = {
										NOT = { has_country_flag = miaphysite_doctrine_sonsofgrace }
										any_owned_province = { has_province_modifier = monastery_unity }
										any_owned_province = { has_province_modifier = monastery_sonsofgrace }
										any_owned_province = { has_province_modifier = monastery_unctionist }
										any_owned_province = { has_province_modifier = monastery_stephanite }
									}
								}
								set_country_flag = miaphysite_controversy
								set_country_flag = miaphysite_controversy_christology
							}
						}
						if = {
							limit = { has_country_flag = miaphysite_controversy }
							clr_country_flag = miaphysite_controversy
							clr_country_flag = miaphysite_controversy_christology
							clr_country_flag = miaphysite_controversy_icons
							clr_country_flag = miaphysite_controversy_sabbath
							if = {
								limit = {
									OR = {
										ai = yes
										has_country_flag = religious_news_trivial
									}
								}
								country_event = { id = dg_miaphysite.123 }
							}
							if = {
								limit = {
									ai = no
									NOT = { has_country_flag = religious_news_trivial }
								}
								if = {
									limit = { piety = 0.60 }
									add_country_modifier = { name = religious_controversy duration = 2500 }
								}
								else_if = {
									limit = { piety = 0.20 }
									add_country_modifier = { name = religious_controversy duration = 2000 }
								}
								else_if = {
									limit = { piety = -0.20 }
									add_country_modifier = { name = religious_controversy duration = 1500 }
								}
								else_if = {
									limit = { piety = -0.60 }
									add_country_modifier = { name = religious_controversy duration = 1000 }
								}
								else = {
									add_country_modifier = { name = religious_controversy duration = 500 }
								}
							}
						}
					}
				}
				#Unusual events
				6 = { #Disciples of Idolators
					random_owned_province = {
						limit = {
							has_province_flag = disbanded_monastery
							NOT = { has_province_modifier = monastery_fortified }
						}
						if = {
							limit = {
								owner = {
									OR = {
										ai = yes
										has_country_flag = religious_news_trivial
									}
								}
							}
							province_event = { id = dg_miaphysite.133 }
						}
						if = {
							limit = { owner = { ai = no NOT = { has_country_flag = religious_news_trivial } } }
							clr_province_flag = disbanded_monastery
							change_variable = { which = province_religion value = -4 }
							change_variable = { which = heretics value = 4 }
						}
					}
				}
				6 = { #Writings of the Negus
					if = {
						limit = {
							has_country_flag = sainted_ruler
							NOT = { has_country_flag = miaphysite_writings }
							OR = { has_regency = no has_consort_regency = yes }
							OR = {
								ADM = 5
								advisor = theologian
							}
						}
						if = {
							limit = {
								OR = {
									ai = yes
									has_country_flag = religious_news_trivial
								}
							}
							country_event = { id = dg_miaphysite.150 }
						}
						if = {
							limit = { ai = no NOT = { has_country_flag = religious_news_trivial } }
							set_country_flag = miaphysite_writings
							dg_add_prestige_small = yes
						}
					}
				}
				6 = { #Icon (not if Stephanites)
					if = {
						limit = {
							at_war_with_religious_enemy = yes
							NOT = { has_country_flag = miaphysite_doctrine_stephanite }
							NOT = { any_owned_province = { has_province_modifier = religious_icon } }
							piety = 0.20
						}
						random_owned_province = {
							limit = {
								OR = {
									is_capital = yes
									has_province_modifier = coptic_pilgrimage
								}
								has_owner_religion = yes
								controlled_by = owner
								has_siege = yes
							}
							if = {
								limit = {
									owner = {
										OR = {
											ai = yes
											has_country_flag = religious_news_major
										}
									}
								}
								province_event = { id = dg_orthodox.011 }
							}
							if = {
								limit = {
									owner = {
										ai = no
										NOT = { has_country_flag = religious_news_major }
									}
								}
								add_province_modifier = { name = religious_icon duration = -1 }
							}
						}
					}
				}
				6 = { #Wandering Debterra
					if = {
						limit = {
							NOT = { has_country_flag = miaphysite_banned_debera }
							NOT = { has_country_modifier = religious_intolerance }
						}
						random_owned_province = {
							limit = {
								has_owner_religion = yes
								has_province_modifier = syncretism
								NOT = { has_province_modifier = religious_scandal_province }
							}
							if = {
								limit = {
									owner = {
										OR = {
											ai = yes
											has_country_flag = religious_news_trivial
										}
									}
								}
								province_event = { id = dg_miaphysite.135 }
							}
							if = {
								limit = { owner = { ai = no NOT = { has_country_flag = religious_news_trivial } } }
								random = {
									chance = 50
									add_province_modifier = { name = religious_scandal_province duration = 1000 }
								}
								random = {
									chance = 50
									hidden_effect = {
										set_variable = { which = added_unrest value = -2 }
										add_base_unrest = yes
									}
									custom_tooltip = added_unrest_2
								}
							}
						}
					}
				}
				6 = { #Hermit
					random_owned_province = {
						limit = {
							has_owner_religion = yes
							OR = {
								AND = {
									town_province_trigger = no #Isolated
									NOT = { any_neighbor_province = { has_province_modifier = monastery_unity } }
									NOT = { any_neighbor_province = { has_province_modifier = monastery_unctionist } }
									NOT = { any_neighbor_province = { has_province_modifier = monastery_zakristos } }
									NOT = { any_neighbor_province = { has_province_modifier = monastery_sonsofgrace } }
									NOT = { any_neighbor_province = { has_province_modifier = monastery_stephanite } }
									NOT = { any_neighbor_province = { has_province_modifier = monastery_fortified } }
								}
								mountains_trigger = yes
								desert_trigger = yes
							}
							NOT = { has_province_modifier = coptic_pilgrimage }
							NOT = { has_province_modifier = monastery_unity }
							NOT = { has_province_modifier = monastery_stephanite }
							NOT = { has_province_modifier = monastery_unctionist }
							NOT = { has_province_modifier = monastery_sonsofgrace }
							NOT = { has_province_modifier = monastery_zakristos }
							NOT = { any_province = { area = PREV has_province_modifier = anchorite_hermitage } }
						}
						if = {
							limit = {
								owner = {
									OR = {
										ai = yes
										has_country_flag = religious_news_trivial
									}
								}
							}
							province_event = { id = dg_miaphysite.122 }
						}
						if = {
							limit = { owner = { ai = no NOT = { has_country_flag = religious_news_trivial } } }
							add_province_modifier = { name = anchorite_hermitage duration = 10000 }
							if = {
								limit = { owner = { piety = 0.60 } }
								random = {
									chance = 50
									add_province_modifier = { name = coptic_pilgrimage duration = 2500 }
								}
							}
							else_if = {
								limit = { owner = { piety = 0.20 } }
								random = {
									chance = 50
									add_province_modifier = { name = coptic_pilgrimage duration = 2000 }
								}
							}
							else_if = {
								limit = { owner = { piety = -0.20 } }
								random = {
									chance = 50
									add_province_modifier = { name = coptic_pilgrimage duration = 1500 }
								}
							}
							else_if = {
								limit = { owner = { piety = -0.60 } }
								random = {
									chance = 50
									add_province_modifier = { name = coptic_pilgrimage duration = 1000 }
								}
							}
							else = {
								random = {
									chance = 50
									add_province_modifier = { name = coptic_pilgrimage duration = 500 }
								}
							}
						}
					}
				}
				6 = { #Our Lady of Lourdes
					random_owned_province = {
						limit = {
							has_owner_religion = yes
							NOT = { has_province_modifier = coptic_pilgrimage }
							NOT = { has_province_modifier = religious_scandal_province }
							NOT = { any_province = { area = PREV has_province_modifier = coptic_pilgrimage } }
						}
						if = {
							limit = {
								owner = {
									OR = {
										ai = yes
										has_country_flag = religious_news_trivial
									}
								}
							}
							province_event = { id = dg_catholic.030 }
						}
						if = {
							limit = {
								owner = {
									ai = no
									NOT = { has_country_flag = religious_news_trivial }
								}
							}
							if = {
								limit = { owner = { piety = 0.60 } }
								add_province_modifier = { name = coptic_pilgrimage duration = 6000 }
							}
							else_if = {
								limit = { owner = { piety = 0.20 } }
								add_province_modifier = { name = coptic_pilgrimage duration = 4500 }
							}
							else_if = {
								limit = { owner = { piety = -0.20 } }
								add_province_modifier = { name = coptic_pilgrimage duration = 3000 }
							}
							else_if = {
								limit = { owner = { NOT = { piety = -0.60 } } }
								add_province_modifier = { name = coptic_pilgrimage duration = 1500 }
							}
						}
					}
				}
				6 = { #Appointing abbots/the ichege
				}
				6 = { #The Holy City of Jerusalem
					if = {
						limit = {
							is_at_war = no
							OR = { has_regency = no has_consort_regency = yes }
							piety = 0.20
						}
						country_event = { id = dg_miaphysite.101 }
					}
				}
			}
		}
	}
	after = {
		dg_patriarch_triggers = yes
	}
}

country_event = { #101 - The Holy City of Jerusalem (1288, 1413)
	
	id = dg_miaphysite.101
	title = dg_miaphysite.101.t
	desc = dg_miaphysite.101.d
	picture = miaphysite_pilgrims_jerusalem_saffron
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	immediate = {
		hidden_effect = {
			ETH = { change_variable = { which = pilgrimages_to_jerusalem value = 1 } }
			if = {
				limit = { NOT = { owns = 379 } }
				#random_country = {
				#	limit = { owns = 379 }
				#	save_event_target_as = jerusalem_host
				#}
				379 = { owner = { save_event_target_as = jerusalem_host } }
				random_known_country = {
					limit = {
						NOT = { border_distance = { who = ROOT distance = 150 } }
						event_target:jerusalem_host = { NOT = { border_distance = { who = PREV distance = 150 } } }
						num_of_ports = 1
					}
					set_country_flag = jerusalem_pilgrimage_far
				}
				if = {
					limit = { NOT = { any_country = { has_country_flag = jerusalem_pilgrimage_far } } }
					random_known_country = {
						limit = {
							NOT = { border_distance = { who = ROOT distance = 150 } }
							event_target:jerusalem_host = { NOT = { border_distance = { who = PREV distance = 150 } } }
						}
						set_country_flag = jerusalem_pilgrimage_far
					}
				}
				random_known_country = {
					limit = {
						NOT = { border_distance = { who = ROOT distance = 75 } }
						event_target:jerusalem_host = { NOT = { border_distance = { who = PREV distance = 75 } } }
						NOT = { has_country_flag = jerusalem_pilgrimage_far }
					}
					set_country_flag = jerusalem_pilgrimage_near
				}
			}
		}
	}
	
	option = {
		name = dg_miaphysite.101.a #Send a bishop in our stead
		ai_chance = { factor = 50 }
		set_country_flag = jerusalem_pilgrimage
		hidden_effect = {
			if = {
				limit = { NOT = { owns = 379 } }
				random_list = {
					15 = {
						set_country_flag = jerusalem_pilgrimage_there

							limit = { has_country_flag = jerusalem_pilgrimage_near }
							country_event = { id = dg_miaphysite.102 days = 60 }
							set_country_flag = jerusalem_pilgrimage_stop
						}
					}
					20 = {
						set_country_flag = jerusalem_pilgrimage_there
						random_known_country = {
							limit = { has_country_flag = jerusalem_pilgrimage_far }
							country_event = { id = dg_miaphysite.102 days = 120 }
							set_country_flag = jerusalem_pilgrimage_stop
						}
					}
					30 = {
						set_country_flag = jerusalem_pilgrimage_there
						#random_country = {
						#	limit = { owns = 379 }
						#	country_event = { id = dg_miaphysite.102 days = 180 }
						#	set_country_flag = jerusalem_pilgrimage_stop
						#}
						379 = {
							owner = {
								country_event = { id = dg_miaphysite.102 days = 180 }
								set_country_flag = jerusalem_pilgrimage_stop
							}
						}
					}
					20 = {
						set_country_flag = jerusalem_pilgrimage_andback
						random_known_country = {
							limit = { has_country_flag = jerusalem_pilgrimage_far }
							country_event = { id = dg_miaphysite.102 days = 240 }
							set_country_flag = jerusalem_pilgrimage_stop
						}
					}
					15 = {
						set_country_flag = jerusalem_pilgrimage_andback
						random_known_country = {
							limit = { has_country_flag = jerusalem_pilgrimage_near }
							country_event = { id = dg_miaphysite.102 days = 300 }
							set_country_flag = jerusalem_pilgrimage_stop
						}
					}
				}
				if = {
					limit = { NOT = { any_country = { has_country_flag = jerusalem_pilgrimage_stop } } }
					country_event = { id = dg_miaphysite.105 days = 180 }
				}
			}
			every_country = {
				clr_country_flag = jerusalem_pilgrimage_near
				clr_country_flag = jerusalem_pilgrimage_far
				clr_country_flag = jerusalem_pilgrimage_stop
			}
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = dg_miaphysite.101.c #Abandon the idea
		ai_chance = { factor = 30 }
		hidden_effect = {
			every_country = {
				clr_country_flag = jerusalem_pilgrimage_near
				clr_country_flag = jerusalem_pilgrimage_far
				clr_country_flag = jerusalem_pilgrimage_stop
			}
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = dg_miaphysite.101.b #Make a personal pilgrimage
		ai_chance = {

			modifier = {

		else = {
			add_country_modifier = { name = jerusalem_pilgrimage duration = 730 }
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			if = {

					15 = {
						set_country_flag = jerusalem_pilgrimage_there

						random_known_country = {
							limit = { has_country_flag = jerusalem_pilgrimage_far }
							country_event = { id = dg_miaphysite.102 days = 120 }
							set_country_flag = jerusalem_pilgrimage_stop
						}
					}
					30 = {
						set_country_flag = jerusalem_pilgrimage_there
						#random_known_country = {
						#	limit = { owns = 379 }
						#	country_event = { id = dg_miaphysite.102 days = 180 }
						#	set_country_flag = jerusalem_pilgrimage_stop
						#}
						379 = {
							owner = {
								country_event = { id = dg_miaphysite.102 days = 180 }
								set_country_flag = jerusalem_pilgrimage_stop
							}
						}
					}
					20 = {
						set_country_flag = jerusalem_pilgrimage_andback
						random_known_country = {
							limit = { has_country_flag = jerusalem_pilgrimage_far }
							country_event = { id = dg_miaphysite.102 days = 240 }
							set_country_flag = jerusalem_pilgrimage_stop
						}
					}
					15 = {
						set_country_flag = jerusalem_pilgrimage_andback
						random_known_country = {
							limit = { has_country_flag = jerusalem_pilgrimage_near }
							country_event = { id = dg_miaphysite.102 days = 300 }
							set_country_flag = jerusalem_pilgrimage_stop
						}
					}
				}
				if = {
					limit = { NOT = { any_country = { has_country_flag = jerusalem_pilgrimage_stop } } }
					country_event = { id = dg_miaphysite.105 days = 180 }
				}
			}
			every_country = {
				clr_country_flag = jerusalem_pilgrimage_near
				clr_country_flag = jerusalem_pilgrimage_far
				clr_country_flag = jerusalem_pilgrimage_stop
			}
		}
	}
}

country_event = { #102 - Notable Pilgrim
	
	id = dg_miaphysite.102
	title = dg_miaphysite.102.t
	desc = dg_miaphysite.102.d
	picture = miaphysite_pilgrims_return_saffron
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	immediate = {
		if = {
			limit = { FROM = { has_country_flag = jerusalem_pilgrimage_there } }
			custom_tooltip = dg_miaphysite.102.there
		}
		if = {
			limit = { FROM = { has_country_flag = jerusalem_pilgrimage_andback } }
			custom_tooltip = dg_miaphysite.102.andback
		}
		if = {
			limit = { FROM = { has_country_modifier = jerusalem_pilgrimage } }
			custom_tooltip = dg_miaphysite.102.ruler
		}
		if = {
			limit = { FROM = { NOT = { has_country_modifier = jerusalem_pilgrimage } } }
			custom_tooltip = dg_miaphysite.102.bishop
		}
	}
	
	option = {
		name = dg_miaphysite.102.e #Let them go
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 20

				FROM = { has_ruler_modifier = jerusalem_pilgrimage }

			}
		}

			limit = { FROM = { NOT = { has_country_modifier = jerusalem_pilgrimage } } }

			limit = { FROM = { has_country_modifier = jerusalem_pilgrimage } }
			FROM = { add_opinion = { who = ROOT modifier = holy_lands_pious } }
		}

		}

			limit = { FROM = { NOT = { has_country_flag = jerusalem_pilgrimage_there } } }

			limit = { FROM = { NOT = { has_country_modifier = jerusalem_pilgrimage } } }

		}
		if = {
			limit = { FROM = { has_country_modifier = jerusalem_pilgrimage } }
			if = {
				limit = {
					FROM = {
						OR = {
							NOT = { num_of_cities = ROOT }
							is_subject_other_than_tributary_trigger = yes
						}
					}
				}
				add_prestige = 2
				FROM = { add_opinion = { who = ROOT modifier = holy_lands_fanatical } }
			}
			if = {

						is_subject_other_than_tributary_trigger = no
					}
				}
				add_prestige = 4
				FROM = { add_opinion = { who = ROOT modifier = holy_lands_fanatical } }
			}
		}
		if = { #Maximum
			limit = { monthly_income = 48 }

		}

		}
		else = { #Minimum
			add_treasury = -1
		}
		if = {
			limit = { FROM = { has_country_flag = jerusalem_pilgrimage_there } }

				set_country_flag = jerusalem_pilgrimage_good

			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = { FROM = { NOT = { has_country_flag = jerusalem_pilgrimage_there } } }
			FROM = {
				set_country_flag = jerusalem_pilgrimage_good
				country_event = { id = dg_miaphysite.105 days = 60 }
			}
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = dg_miaphysite.102.g #Extort them
		trigger = {
			FROM = { NOT = { overlord_of = ROOT } }
			FROM = { NOT = { is_subject_of = ROOT } }
		}

			factor = 20
			modifier = {

			}
			modifier = {

				factor = 0.5

		}
	}

country_event = { #103 - Prisoner of the [Sultan]
	
	id = dg_miaphysite.103
	title = dg_miaphysite.103.t
	desc = dg_miaphysite.103.d
	picture = miaphysite_noble_arrest_saffron
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	immediate = {
		if = {
			limit = { has_country_modifier = jerusalem_pilgrimage }
			set_country_flag = captive_ruler
			exile_ruler_as = captive_pilgrim
		}
	}
	
	option = {
		name = dg_miaphysite.103.a #Pay the ransom
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 50
			modifier = {
				has_country_modifier = jerusalem_pilgrimage
				ADM = 5
				factor = 0.7
			}
			modifier = {
				has_country_modifier = jerusalem_pilgrimage
				ADM = 6
				factor = 0.7
			}
			modifier = {
				has_country_modifier = jerusalem_pilgrimage
				MIL = 5
				factor = 0.7
			}
			modifier = {
				has_country_modifier = jerusalem_pilgrimage
				MIL = 6
				factor = 0.7
			}
			modifier = {
				has_country_modifier = jerusalem_pilgrimage
				DIP = 5
				factor = 0.7
			}
			modifier = {
				has_country_modifier = jerusalem_pilgrimage
				DIP = 6
				factor = 0.7
			}
			modifier = {
				has_country_modifier = jerusalem_pilgrimage
				NOT = { ADM = 2 }
				factor = 2
			}
			modifier = {
				has_country_modifier = jerusalem_pilgrimage
				NOT = { ADM = 1 }
				factor = 2
			}
			modifier = {
				has_country_modifier = jerusalem_pilgrimage
				NOT = { MIL = 2 }
				factor = 2
			}
			modifier = {
				has_country_modifier = jerusalem_pilgrimage
				NOT = { MIL = 1 }
				factor = 2
			}
			modifier = {
				has_country_modifier = jerusalem_pilgrimage
				NOT = { DIP = 2 }
				factor = 2
			}
			modifier = {
				has_country_modifier = jerusalem_pilgrimage
				NOT = { DIP = 1 }
				factor = 2
			}
		}
		set_country_flag = ransom_paid
		if = {
			limit = { has_country_modifier = jerusalem_pilgrimage }
			set_country_flag = ransomed_ruler
			if = {
				limit = { piety = 0.60 }
				add_prestige = -10
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = { piety = 0.20 }
				add_prestige = -8
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = { piety = -0.20 }
				add_prestige = -6
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = { piety = -0.60 }
				add_prestige = -4
			}
			else = {
				add_prestige = -2
			}
			if = {
				limit = { monthly_income = 50 }
				add_treasury = -200
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = { monthly_income = 25 }
				add_treasury = -100
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = { monthly_income = 10 }
				add_treasury = -50
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = { monthly_income = 5 }
				add_treasury = -25
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = { monthly_income = 2 }
				add_treasury = -10
			}
			else = {
				add_treasury = -5
			}
		}
		else = {
			dg_reduce_prestige_small = yes
			if = {
				limit = { monthly_income = 50 }
				add_treasury = -50
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = { monthly_income = 25 }
				add_treasury = -25
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = { monthly_income = 10 }
				add_treasury = -10
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = { monthly_income = 5 }
				add_treasury = -5
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = { monthly_income = 2 }
				add_treasury = -2
			}
			else = {
				add_treasury = -1
			}
		}
		FROM = { country_event = { id = dg_miaphysite.106 days = 30 } }
	}
	option = {
		name = dg_miaphysite.103.b #Appoint a new bishop
		trigger = { NOT = { has_country_modifier = jerusalem_pilgrimage } }
		ai_chance = { factor = 40 }
		add_adm_power = -5
		if = {
			limit = { patriarch_authority = 0.80 }
			add_country_modifier = { name = unhappy_church_powerful duration = 500 }
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = { patriarch_authority = 0.60 }
			add_country_modifier = { name = unhappy_church_strong duration = 500 }
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = { patriarch_authority = 0.40 }
			add_country_modifier = { name = unhappy_church_moderate duration = 500 }
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = { patriarch_authority = 0.20 }
			add_country_modifier = { name = unhappy_church_weak duration = 500 }
		}
		else = {
			add_country_modifier = { name = unhappy_church_impotent duration = 500 }
		}
		FROM = { country_event = { id = dg_miaphysite.106 days = 30 } }
	}
	option = {
		name = dg_miaphysite.103.c #Appoint a new ruler
		trigger = { has_country_modifier = jerusalem_pilgrimage }
		ai_chance = { factor = 10 }
		add_adm_power = -50
		add_legitimacy = -10
		add_devotion = -10
		add_republican_tradition = -10
		remove_country_modifier = jerusalem_pilgrimage
		FROM = { country_event = { id = dg_miaphysite.106 days = 30 } }
	}
}

country_event = { #104 - The Merciless [Sultan]
	
	id = dg_miaphysite.104
	title = dg_miaphysite.104.t
	desc = dg_miaphysite.104.d
	picture = miaphysite_priest_coffin_saffron
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	immediate = {
		if = {
			limit = {
				NOT = { has_country_flag = captive_ruler }
				NOT = { has_country_modifier = jerusalem_pilgrimage }
			}
			if = {
				limit = { has_country_flag = enslaved_captives }
				custom_tooltip = dg_miaphysite.104.slaves
			}
			else = {
				custom_tooltip = dg_miaphysite.104.death
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					has_country_flag = captive_ruler
					has_country_modifier = jerusalem_pilgrimage
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = { has_country_flag = enslaved_captives }
				custom_tooltip = dg_miaphysite.104.ruler_slaves
			}
			else = {
				custom_tooltip = dg_miaphysite.104.ruler_death
			}
		}
	}
	
	option = {
		name = dg_miaphysite.104.a
		clr_country_flag = enslaved_captives
		add_prestige = -10
		if = {
			limit = {
				NOT = { has_country_flag = captive_ruler }
				NOT = { has_country_modifier = jerusalem_pilgrimage }
			}
			reverse_add_opinion = { who = FROM modifier = mistreated_coreligionists_pious }
			add_casus_belli = { type = cb_insult target = FROM months = 60 }
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					has_country_flag = captive_ruler
					has_country_modifier = jerusalem_pilgrimage
				}
			}
			clr_country_flag = captive_ruler
			reverse_add_opinion = { who = FROM modifier = mistreated_coreligionists_fanatical }
			add_casus_belli = { type = cb_insult target = FROM months = 240 }
		}
		if = {
			limit = { has_country_modifier = jerusalem_pilgrimage }
			kill_ruler = yes
		}
		clr_country_flag = jerusalem_pilgrimage_good
		clr_country_flag = jerusalem_pilgrimage_bad
		clr_country_flag = jerusalem_pilgrimage_there
		clr_country_flag = jerusalem_pilgrimage_andback
		clr_country_flag = pilgrim_converted
		clr_country_flag = ransom_paid
		clr_country_flag = ransomed_ruler
		clr_country_flag = captive_ruler
	}
}

	title = dg_miaphysite.105.t
	desc = dg_miaphysite.105.d

				}

			}
			if = {

			}
		}
	}
	
	option = {
		name = dg_miaphysite.105.a
		trigger = {
			OR = {
				NOT = { has_country_flag = pilgrim_converted }
				NOT = { has_country_modifier = jerusalem_pilgrimage }
			}
		}
		ai_chance = { factor = 50 }
		if = {
			limit = { has_country_flag = captive_ruler }
			clr_country_flag = captive_ruler
			set_ruler = captive_pilgrim
			add_stability_1 = yes
		}
		if = {
			limit = { NOT = { has_country_modifier = jerusalem_pilgrimage } }
			dg_add_prestige_small = yes
			if = {
				limit = { has_country_flag = jerusalem_pilgrimage_good }
				add_opinion = { who = FROM modifier = holy_lands_observant }
			}
			if = {
				limit = { has_country_flag = jerusalem_pilgrimage_bad }
				add_opinion = { who = FROM modifier = mistreated_coreligionists_decadent }
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = { has_country_modifier = jerusalem_pilgrimage }
			remove_country_modifier = jerusalem_pilgrimage
			if = {
				limit = { piety = 0.60 }
				add_prestige = 10
				add_legitimacy = 5
				add_republican_tradition = 2.5
				add_devotion = 10
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = { piety = 0.20 }
				add_prestige = 8
				add_legitimacy = 4
				add_republican_tradition = 2
				add_devotion = 8
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = { piety = -0.20 }
				add_prestige = 6
				add_legitimacy = 3
				add_republican_tradition = 1.5
				add_devotion = 6
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = { piety = -0.60 }
				add_prestige = 4
				add_legitimacy = 2
				add_republican_tradition = 1
				add_devotion = 4
			}
			else = {
				add_prestige = 2
				add_legitimacy = 1
				add_republican_tradition = 0.5
				add_devotion = 2
			}
			if = {
				limit = { has_country_flag = jerusalem_pilgrimage_good }
				add_opinion = { who = FROM modifier = holy_lands_pious }
			}
			if = {
				limit = { has_country_flag = jerusalem_pilgrimage_bad }
				add_opinion = { who = FROM modifier = mistreated_coreligionists_observant }
			}
		}
		clr_country_flag = jerusalem_pilgrimage_good
		clr_country_flag = jerusalem_pilgrimage_bad
		clr_country_flag = jerusalem_pilgrimage_there
		clr_country_flag = jerusalem_pilgrimage_andback
		clr_country_flag = pilgrim_converted
		clr_country_flag = ransom_paid
		clr_country_flag = ransomed_ruler
		clr_country_flag = captive_ruler
	}
	option = {
		name = dg_miaphysite.105.b #Stay true to the faith
		trigger = {
			has_country_flag = pilgrim_converted
			has_country_modifier = jerusalem_pilgrimage
		}
		ai_chance = { factor = 40 }
		remove_country_modifier = jerusalem_pilgrimage
		dg_add_legitimacy = yes
		if = {
			limit = { piety = 0.60 }
			add_prestige = 10
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = { piety = 0.20 }
			add_prestige = 8
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = { piety = -0.20 }
			add_prestige = 6
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = { piety = -0.60 }
			add_prestige = 4
		}
		else = {
			add_prestige = 2
		}
		add_opinion = { who = FROM modifier = mistreated_coreligionists_pious }
		clr_country_flag = jerusalem_pilgrimage_good
		clr_country_flag = jerusalem_pilgrimage_bad
		clr_country_flag = jerusalem_pilgrimage_there
		clr_country_flag = jerusalem_pilgrimage_andback
		clr_country_flag = pilgrim_converted
		clr_country_flag = ransom_paid
		clr_country_flag = ransomed_ruler
		clr_country_flag = captive_ruler
	}
	option = {
		name = dg_miaphysite.105.c #Convert
		trigger = {
			has_country_flag = pilgrim_converted
			has_country_modifier = jerusalem_pilgrimage
		}
		ai_chance = { factor = 10 }
		remove_country_modifier = jerusalem_pilgrimage
		subtract_stability_5 = yes
		if = {
			limit = { FROM = { religion = sunni } }
			change_religion = sunni
		}
		if = {
			limit = { FROM = { religion = shiite } }
			change_religion = shiite
		}
		if = {
			limit = { FROM = { religion = druze } }
			change_religion = druze
		}
		if = {
			limit = { FROM = { religion = ibadi } }
			change_religion = ibadi
		}
		if = {
			limit = { FROM = { religion = wahhabi } }
			change_religion = wahhabi
		}
		if = {
			limit = { FROM = { religion = jewish } }
			change_religion = jewish
		}
		if = {
			limit = { FROM = { religion = catholic } }
			change_religion = catholic
		}
		if = {
			limit = { FROM = { religion = orthodox } }
			change_religion = orthodox
		}
		if = {
			limit = { FROM = { religion = chaldean } }
			change_religion = chaldean
		}
		if = {
			limit = { FROM = { religion = gnostic } }
			change_religion = gnostic
		}
		if = {
			limit = { FROM = { religion = protestant } }
			change_religion = protestant
		}
		if = {

			change_religion = reformed

		clr_country_flag = jerusalem_pilgrimage_good

country_event = { #106 - [Ethiopian] Response
	
	id = dg_miaphysite.106
	title = dg_miaphysite.106.t
	desc = dg_miaphysite.106.d
	picture = miaphysite_imperial_decree_saffron
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	immediate = {
		if = {
			limit = { FROM = { NOT = { has_country_flag = ransom_paid } } }
			custom_tooltip = dg_miaphysite.106.d_unpaid
		}
		if = {
			limit = { FROM = { has_country_flag = ransom_paid } }
			custom_tooltip = dg_miaphysite.106.d_paid
			if = {
				limit = { FROM = { NOT = { has_country_flag = ransomed_ruler } } }
				if = {
					limit = { FROM = { monthly_income = 50 } }
					add_treasury = 50
				}
				else_if = {
					limit = { FROM = { monthly_income = 25 } }
					add_treasury = 25
				}
				else_if = {
					limit = { FROM = { monthly_income = 10 } }
					add_treasury = 10
				}
				else_if = {
					limit = { FROM = { monthly_income = 5 } }
					add_treasury = 5
				}
				else_if = {
					limit = { FROM = { monthly_income = 2 } }
					add_treasury = 2
				}
				else = {
					add_treasury = 1
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = { FROM = { has_country_flag = ransomed_ruler } }
				if = {
					limit = { FROM = { monthly_income = 50 } }
					add_treasury = 200
				}
				else_if = {
					limit = { FROM = { monthly_income = 25 } }
					add_treasury = 100
				}
				else_if = {
					limit = { FROM = { monthly_income = 10 } }
					add_treasury = 50
				}
				else_if = {
					limit = { FROM = { monthly_income = 5 } }
					add_treasury = 25
				}
				else_if = {
					limit = { FROM = { monthly_income = 2 } }
					add_treasury = 10
				}
				else = {
					add_treasury = 5
				}
			}
		}
	}
	
	option = {
		name = dg_miaphysite.106.a #Let them go
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 70
			modifier = {
				FROM = { army_size = ROOT }
				factor = 2
			}
			modifier = {
				FROM = { is_rival = ROOT }
				factor = 0.5
			}
			modifier = {
				FROM = { is_enemy = ROOT }
				factor = 0.5
			}
			modifier = {
				FROM = { religion = ROOT }
				factor = 2
			}
			modifier = {
				FROM = { war_with = ROOT }
				factor = 0.5
			}
			modifier = {
				FROM = { NOT = { has_country_flag = ransom_paid } }
				factor = 0.5
			}
		}
		FROM = {
			clr_country_flag = jerusalem_pilgrimage_good
			set_country_flag = jerusalem_pilgrimage_bad
			country_event = { id = dg_miaphysite.105 days = 30 }
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = dg_miaphysite.106.b #Sell them into slavery
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 20
			modifier = {
				FROM = { NOT = { has_country_flag = ransom_paid } }
				factor = 2
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = { FROM = { has_country_flag = ransom_paid } }
			add_legitimacy = -5
			add_devotion = -5
			add_republican_tradition = -5
		}
		FROM = {
			country_event = { id = dg_miaphysite.104 days = 30 }
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = dg_miaphysite.106.c #Execute them
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 10
			modifier = {
				FROM = { NOT = { has_country_flag = ransom_paid } }
				factor = 2
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = { FROM = { has_country_flag = ransom_paid } }
			add_legitimacy = -5
			add_devotion = -5
			add_republican_tradition = -5
		}
		FROM = {
			country_event = { id = dg_miaphysite.104 days = 30 }
		}
	}
}

country_event = { #107 - Canonization of the [Negus]
	
	id = dg_miaphysite.107
	title = dg_miaphysite.107.t
	desc = dg_miaphysite.107.d
	picture = miaphysite_priest_coffin_saffron
	
	is_triggered_only = yes #Upon new ruler with sainted ruler and obedient patriarch
	
	option = {
		name = dg_miaphysite.107.a #Yes, canonize him
		ai_chance = { factor = 99 }
		add_adm_power = -25
		add_stability_1 = yes
		if = {
			limit = { piety = 0.60 }
			add_prestige = 20
			add_devotion = 20
		}
		else = {
			add_prestige = 10
			add_devotion = 10
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = dg_miaphysite.107.b
		trigger = { NOT = { government = theocracy } }
		ai_chance = { factor = 1 } #No, do not tie ourselves to the Church
		if = {
			limit = { piety = 0.60 }
			add_legitimacy = 2
			add_republican_tradition = 2
		}
		else = {
			add_legitimacy = 4
			add_republican_tradition = 4
		}
	}
}

	immediate = {

			}
			modifier = {
				owner = {
					has_country_flag = monastery_zakristos
					has_country_flag = persecuted_zakristos
				}
				factor = 0.5
			}
			modifier = {
				owner = {
					has_country_flag = monastery_stephanite
					has_country_flag = persecuted_stephanite
				}
				factor = 0.5
			}
		}
		owner = {
			if = {
				limit = { has_country_flag = monastery_unity }
				every_owned_province = {
					limit = { has_province_flag = event_target }
					add_province_modifier = { name = monastery_unity duration = 10000 }
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = { has_country_flag = monastery_unctionist }
				every_owned_province = {
					limit = { has_province_flag = event_target }
					add_province_modifier = { name = monastery_unctionist duration = 10000 }
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = { has_country_flag = monastery_sonsofgrace }
				every_owned_province = {
					limit = { has_province_flag = event_target }
					add_province_modifier = { name = monastery_sonsofgrace duration = 10000 }
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = { has_country_flag = monastery_zakristos }
				every_owned_province = {
					limit = { has_province_flag = event_target }
					add_province_modifier = { name = monastery_zakristos duration = 10000 }
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = { has_country_flag = monastery_stephanite }
				every_owned_province = {
					limit = { has_province_flag = event_target }
					add_province_modifier = { name = monastery_stephanite duration = 10000 }
				}
			}
			every_owned_province = { clr_province_flag = event_target }
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = dg_miaphysite.121.b #Persecute them
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 20
			modifier = {
				owner = {
					has_country_flag = monastery_unity
					has_country_flag = persecuted_unity
				}
				factor = 2
			}
			modifier = {
				owner = {
					has_country_flag = monastery_unctionist
					has_country_flag = persecuted_unctionist
				}
				factor = 2
			}
			modifier = {
				owner = {
					has_country_flag = monastery_sonsofgrace
					has_country_flag = persecuted_sonsofgrace
				}
				factor = 2
			}
			modifier = {
				owner = {
					has_country_flag = monastery_zakristos
					has_country_flag = persecuted_zakristos
				}
				factor = 2
			}
			modifier = {
				owner = {
					has_country_flag = monastery_stephanite
					has_country_flag = persecuted_stephanite
				}
				factor = 2
			}
		}
		trigger = {
			owner = {
				NOT = { has_country_flag = patriarch_hostile }
				NOT = { has_country_flag = patriarch_theologian }
				OR = {
					AND = {
						NOT = { has_country_flag = miaphysite_doctrine_unctionist }
						NOT = { has_country_flag = miaphysite_doctrine_sonsofgrace }
						NOT = { has_country_flag = miaphysite_doctrine_zakristos }
						NOT = { has_country_flag = miaphysite_doctrine_stephanite }
						NOT = { has_country_flag = monastery_unity }
					}
					AND = {
						has_country_flag = miaphysite_doctrine_unctionist
						NOT = { has_country_flag = monastery_unctionist }
					}
					AND = {
						has_country_flag = miaphysite_doctrine_sonsofgrace
						NOT = { has_country_flag = monastery_sonsofgrace }
					}
					AND = {
						has_country_flag = miaphysite_doctrine_zakristos
						NOT = { has_country_flag = monastery_zakristos }
					}
					AND = {
						has_country_flag = miaphysite_doctrine_stephanite
						NOT = { has_country_flag = monastery_stephanite }
					}
				}
			}
		}
		owner = {
			add_adm_power = -10
			if = {
				limit = { has_country_flag = monastery_unity }
				every_owned_province = {
					limit = {
						OR = {
							has_province_flag = event_target
							has_province_modifier = monastery_unity
						}
					}
					hidden_effect = {
						set_variable = { which = added_unrest value = 3 }
						add_base_unrest = yes
					}
					custom_tooltip = added_unrest_3
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = { has_country_flag = monastery_unctionist }
				every_owned_province = {
					limit = {
						OR = {
							has_province_flag = event_target
							has_province_modifier = monastery_unctionist
						}
					}
					hidden_effect = {
						set_variable = { which = added_unrest value = 3 }
						add_base_unrest = yes
					}
					custom_tooltip = added_unrest_3
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = { has_country_flag = monastery_sonsofgrace }
				every_owned_province = {
					limit = {
						OR = {
							has_province_flag = event_target
							has_province_modifier = monastery_sonsofgrace
						}
					}
					hidden_effect = {
						set_variable = { which = added_unrest value = 3 }
						add_base_unrest = yes
					}
					custom_tooltip = added_unrest_3
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = { has_country_flag = monastery_zakristos }
				every_owned_province = {
					limit = {
						OR = {
							has_province_flag = event_target
							has_province_modifier = monastery_zakristos
						}
					}
					hidden_effect = {
						set_variable = { which = added_unrest value = 3 }
						add_base_unrest = yes
					}
					custom_tooltip = added_unrest_3
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = { has_country_flag = monastery_stephanite }
				every_owned_province = {
					limit = {
						OR = {
							has_province_flag = event_target
							has_province_modifier = monastery_stephanite
							has_province_modifier = monastery_fortified
						}
					}
					hidden_effect = {
						set_variable = { which = added_unrest value = 3 }
						add_base_unrest = yes
					}
					custom_tooltip = added_unrest_3
				}
				if = {
					limit = { NOT = { has_country_flag = miaphysite_stephanite_banned } }
					country_event = { id = dg_miaphysite.132 }
				}
			}
			every_owned_province = { clr_province_flag = event_target }
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = dg_miaphysite.121.c #Criticize monasticism
		ai_chance = { factor = 5 }
		trigger = {
			owner = {
				OR = {
					AND = {
						NOT = { has_country_flag = miaphysite_doctrine_unctionist }
						NOT = { has_country_flag = miaphysite_doctrine_sonsofgrace }
						NOT = { has_country_flag = miaphysite_doctrine_zakristos }
						NOT = { has_country_flag = miaphysite_doctrine_stephanite }
						has_country_flag = monastery_unity
					}
					AND = {
						has_country_flag = miaphysite_doctrine_unctionist
						has_country_flag = monastery_unctionist
					}
					AND = {
						has_country_flag = miaphysite_doctrine_sonsofgrace
						has_country_flag = monastery_sonsofgrace
					}
					AND = {
						has_country_flag = miaphysite_doctrine_zakristos
						has_country_flag = monastery_zakristos
					}
					AND = {
						has_country_flag = miaphysite_doctrine_stephanite
						has_country_flag = monastery_stephanite
					}
				}
			}
		}
		owner = {
			add_adm_power = -25
			every_owned_province = {
				clr_province_flag = event_target
			}
		}
		hidden_effect = { change_variable = { which = monastic_decline value = 1 } }
		custom_tooltip = monastic_decline_explained
		if = {
			limit = { NOT = { has_country_flag = patriarch_hostile } }
			random = {
				chance = 50
				custom_tooltip = patriarch_becomes_hostile
				set_country_flag = patriarch_hostile
				clr_country_flag = patriarch_controversial
				clr_country_flag = patriarch_zealous
				clr_country_flag = patriarch_obedient
				clr_country_flag = patriarch_theologian
				clr_country_flag = patriarch_corrupt
			}
		}
	}
}

		}
		if = {
			limit = { has_country_flag = miaphysite_controversy_christology }

				limit = { has_country_flag = miaphysite_doctrine_unctionist }

				}

					limit = { any_owned_province = { has_province_modifier = monastery_sonsofgrace } }
					custom_tooltip = dg_miaphysite.123.christology_minority_sonsofgrace
				}
				if = {
					limit = { any_owned_province = { has_province_modifier = monastery_zakristos } }
					custom_tooltip = dg_miaphysite.123.christology_minority_zakristos
				}

			if = {
				limit = { has_country_flag = miaphysite_doctrine_sonsofgrace }

					custom_tooltip = dg_miaphysite.123.christology_minority_unctionist
				}
				if = {
					limit = { any_owned_province = { has_province_modifier = monastery_zakristos } }
					custom_tooltip = dg_miaphysite.123.christology_minority_zakristos
				}

			if = {
				limit = { has_country_flag = miaphysite_doctrine_zakristos }

					custom_tooltip = dg_miaphysite.123.christology_minority_unity
				}
				if = {
					limit = { any_owned_province = { has_province_modifier = monastery_unctionist } }
					custom_tooltip = dg_miaphysite.123.christology_minority_unctionist
				}
				if = {
					limit = { any_owned_province = { has_province_modifier = monastery_sonsofgrace } }
					custom_tooltip = dg_miaphysite.123.christology_minority_sonsofgrace
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					NOT = { has_country_flag = miaphysite_doctrine_sonsofgrace }
					NOT = { has_country_flag = miaphysite_doctrine_unctionist }
					NOT = { has_country_flag = miaphysite_doctrine_zakristos }
				}
				custom_tooltip = dg_miaphysite.123.christology_unity
				if = {
					limit = { any_owned_province = { has_province_modifier = monastery_unctionist } }
					custom_tooltip = dg_miaphysite.123.christology_minority_unctionist
				}
				if = {
					limit = { any_owned_province = { has_province_modifier = monastery_sonsofgrace } }
					custom_tooltip = dg_miaphysite.123.christology_minority_sonsofgrace
				}
				if = {
					limit = { any_owned_province = { has_province_modifier = monastery_zakristos } }
					custom_tooltip = dg_miaphysite.123.christology_minority_zakristos

			limit = { piety = 0.60 }

			limit = { piety = 0.20 }

			limit = { piety = -0.60 }
			add_country_modifier = { name = religious_controversy duration = 1000 }
		}

			add_country_modifier = { name = religious_controversy duration = 500 }
		}

	option = {

			}
			province_event = { id = dg_miaphysite.125 days = 90 }
		}
	}
}

country_event = { #124 - The Children of Grace (1750)
	
	id = dg_miaphysite.124
	title = dg_miaphysite.124.t
	desc = dg_miaphysite.124.d
	picture = miaphysite_patriarch_argument_saffron
	
	trigger = {
		has_country_flag = synod_over
		has_country_flag = miaphysite_controversy_christology
		NOT = { has_country_flag = sonsofgrace_origins }
	}
	
	mean_time_to_happen = { months = 6 }
	
	immediate = {
		set_country_flag = sonsofgrace_foundation
		set_country_flag = sonsofgrace_origins
		hidden_effect = {
			random_owned_province = {
				limit = { has_owner_religion = yes }
				set_province_flag = sonsofgrace
			}
			if = {
				limit = { has_country_flag = miaphysite_doctrine_zakristos }
				every_owned_province = {
					limit = { has_province_modifier = monastery_zakristos }
					random = { chance = 40 set_province_flag = sonsofgrace }
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = { has_country_flag = miaphysite_doctrine_stephanite }
				every_owned_province = {
					limit = { has_province_modifier = monastery_stephanite }
					random = { chance = 40 set_province_flag = sonsofgrace }
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = { has_country_flag = miaphysite_doctrine_unctionist }
				every_owned_province = {
					limit = { has_province_modifier = monastery_unctionist }
					random = { chance = 40 set_province_flag = sonsofgrace }
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					NOT = { has_country_flag = miaphysite_doctrine_zakristos }
					NOT = { has_country_flag = miaphysite_doctrine_stephanite }
					NOT = { has_country_flag = miaphysite_doctrine_unctionist }
				}
				every_owned_province = {
					limit = { has_province_modifier = monastery_unity }
					random = { chance = 40 set_province_flag = sonsofgrace }
				}
			}
			random_owned_province = {
				limit = {
					has_province_flag = sonsofgrace
					NOT = { has_province_flag = unity_center }
					NOT = { has_province_flag = unctionist_center }
					NOT = { has_province_flag = zakristos_center }
					NOT = { has_province_flag = stephanite_center }
				}
				set_province_flag = sonsofgrace_center
			}
		}
	}
	
	option = {
		name = dg_miaphysite.124.a #Find a peaceful solution
		ai_chance = { factor = 70 }
		every_owned_province = {
			limit = { has_province_flag = sonsofgrace }
			clr_province_flag = sonsofgrace
			remove_province_modifier = monastery_stephanite
			remove_province_modifier = monastery_unctionist
			remove_province_modifier = monastery_zakristos
			remove_province_modifier = monastery_unity
			add_province_modifier = { name = monastery_sonsofgrace duration = 10000 }
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = dg_miaphysite.124.b #Declare them to be heretics
		ai_chance = { factor = 30 }
		set_country_flag = miaphysite_sonsofgrace_banned
		every_owned_province = {
			limit = { has_province_flag = sonsofgrace }
			clr_province_flag = sonsofgrace
			hidden_effect = {
				set_variable = { which = added_unrest value = 10 }
				add_base_unrest = yes
			}
			custom_tooltip = added_unrest_10
			remove_province_modifier = monastery_stephanite
			remove_province_modifier = monastery_unctionist
			remove_province_modifier = monastery_zakristos
			remove_province_modifier = monastery_unity
			random = {
				chance = 40
				add_province_modifier = { name = monastery_fortified duration = 20000 }
				set_province_flag = disbanded_monastery
			}
		}
	}
}

province_event = { #125 - Synod of [Debre Mitmaq] (1450)
	
	id = dg_miaphysite.125
	title = dg_miaphysite.125.t
	desc = dg_miaphysite.125.d
	picture = miaphysite_bishops_emperor_saffron

	option = {
		name = dg_miaphysite.125.compromise #Forge a compromise
		ai_chance = { factor = 30 }
		owner = {
			add_adm_power = -10
			set_country_flag = synod_over
			set_country_flag = synod_compromise
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = dg_miaphysite.125.state #Side with the State Church
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 20
			modifier = {
				owner = {
					OR = {
						has_country_modifier = unhappy_church_powerful
						has_country_modifier = unhappy_church_strong
						has_country_modifier = unhappy_church_moderate
						has_country_modifier = unhappy_church_weak
						has_country_modifier = unhappy_church_impotent
					}
				}
				factor = 2
			}
		}
		owner = {
			set_country_flag = synod_over
			trigger_switch = {
				on_trigger = has_country_modifier
				unhappy_church_powerful = {
					remove_country_modifier = unhappy_church_powerful
				}
				unhappy_church_strong = {
					remove_country_modifier = unhappy_church_strong
				}
				unhappy_church_moderate = {
					remove_country_modifier = unhappy_church_moderate
				}
				unhappy_church_weak = {
					remove_country_modifier = unhappy_church_weak
				}
				unhappy_church_impotent = {
					remove_country_modifier = unhappy_church_impotent
				}
			}
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = dg_miaphysite.125.unity
		trigger = {
			owner = {
				any_owned_province = { has_province_modifier = monastery_unity }
				NOT = { has_country_flag = miaphysite_unity_banned }
				OR = {
					has_country_flag = miaphysite_doctrine_zakristos
					has_country_flag = miaphysite_doctrine_unctionist
					has_country_flag = miaphysite_doctrine_sonsofgrace
					has_country_flag = miaphysite_doctrine_stephanite
				}
			}
		}
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 10
		}
		owner = {
			dg_reduce_legitimacy = yes
			if = {
				limit = { piety = 0.60 }
				add_country_modifier = { name = religious_controversy duration = 5000 }
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = { piety = 0.20 }
				add_country_modifier = { name = religious_controversy duration = 4000 }
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = { piety = -0.20 }
				add_country_modifier = { name = religious_controversy duration = 3000 }
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = { piety = -0.60 }
				add_country_modifier = { name = religious_controversy duration = 2000 }
			}
			else = {
				add_country_modifier = { name = religious_controversy duration = 1000 }
			}
			custom_tooltip = changes_dominant_sect
			set_country_flag = synod_over
			clr_country_flag = miaphysite_doctrine_unctionist
			clr_country_flag = miaphysite_doctrine_zakristos
			clr_country_flag = miaphysite_doctrine_sonsofgrace
			clr_country_flag = miaphysite_doctrine_stephanite
			hidden_effect = { set_variable = { which = miaphysite_unity_blamed value = 0 } }
		}
	}
	option = {

		trigger = {
			owner = {
				any_owned_province = { has_province_modifier = monastery_unctionist }

country_event = { #126 - Lasting compromise
	
	id = dg_miaphysite.126
	title = dg_miaphysite.126.t
	desc = dg_miaphysite.126.d
	picture = miaphysite_imperial_decree_saffron
	
	trigger = {
		has_country_flag = synod_compromise
		NOT = { has_country_flag = patriarch_hostile }
	}
	
	mean_time_to_happen = {
		
		months = 9
		
		modifier = {
			has_country_flag = patriarch_controversial
			factor = 3
		}
		modifier = {
			has_country_flag = patriarch_corrupt
			factor = 3
		}
		modifier = {
			has_country_flag = patriarch_theologian
			factor = 0.7
		}
		modifier = {
			theologian = 2
			factor = 0.7
		}
		modifier = {
			ADM = 5
			factor = 0.7
		}
		modifier = {
			NOT = { ADM = 2 }
			factor = 2
		}
		modifier = {
			has_country_flag = miaphysite_controversy_sabbath_resolved
			factor = 1.4
		}
		modifier = {
			has_country_flag = miaphysite_controversy_icons_resolved
			factor = 1.4
		}
		modifier = {
			has_country_flag = miaphysite_controversy_christology_resolved
			factor = 1.4
		}
		modifier = {
			has_country_flag = miaphysite_controversy_christology
			NOT = { has_country_flag = sonsofgrace_foundation }
			factor = 1.4
		}
	}
	
	immediate = {
		clr_country_flag = synod_over
		clr_country_flag = synod_compromise
		if = {
			limit = { has_country_flag = miaphysite_controversy_sabbath }
			custom_tooltip = dg_miaphysite.126.sabbath
		}
		if = {
			limit = { has_country_flag = miaphysite_controversy_christology }
			custom_tooltip = dg_miaphysite.126.christology
		}
		if = {
			limit = { has_country_flag = miaphysite_controversy_icons }
			custom_tooltip = dg_miaphysite.126.icons
		}
	}
	
	option = {
		name = dg_miaphysite.126.a
		if = {
			limit = { piety = 0.60 }
			add_prestige = 20
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = { piety = 0.20 }
			add_prestige = 16
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = { piety = -0.20 }
			add_prestige = 12
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = { piety = -0.60 }
			add_prestige = 8
		}
		else = {
			add_prestige = 4
		}
		if = {
			limit = { has_country_flag = miaphysite_controversy_sabbath }
			set_country_flag = miaphysite_controversy_sabbath_resolved
		}
		if = {
			limit = { has_country_flag = miaphysite_controversy_christology }
			set_country_flag = miaphysite_controversy_christology_resolved
		}
		if = {
			limit = { has_country_flag = miaphysite_controversy_icons }
			set_country_flag = miaphysite_controversy_icons_resolved
		}
		clr_country_flag = miaphysite_controversy_sabbath
		clr_country_flag = miaphysite_controversy_christology
		clr_country_flag = miaphysite_controversy_icons
	}
}
