country_event = { #128 - Imperial Decree (only once per ruler)
	
	id = dg_miaphysite.128
	title = dg_miaphysite.128.t
	desc = dg_miaphysite.128.d
	picture = miaphysite_imperial_decree_saffron
	
	trigger = {
		religion = coptic
		NOT = { has_country_flag = miaphysite_monks_exiled }
		OR = {
			check_variable = { which = miaphysite_unity_blamed value = 3 }
			check_variable = { which = miaphysite_unctionist_blamed value = 3 }
			check_variable = { which = miaphysite_zakristos_blamed value = 3 }
			check_variable = { which = miaphysite_stephanite_blamed value = 3 }
			check_variable = { which = miaphysite_sonsofgrace_blamed value = 3 }
		}
		is_at_war = no
		OR = { has_regency = no has_consort_regency = yes }
		has_any_disaster = no
	}
	
	mean_time_to_happen = { months = 6 }
	
	immediate = { set_country_flag = miaphysite_monks_exiled }
	
	option = {
		name = dg_miaphysite.128.a #Back down
		ai_chance = { factor = 10 }
		add_prestige = 1
		hidden_effect = {
			if = {
				limit = { check_variable = { which = miaphysite_unity_blamed value = 3 } }
				change_variable = { which = miaphysite_unity_blamed value = -1 }
			}
			if = {
				limit = { check_variable = { which = miaphysite_unctionist_blamed value = 3 } }
				change_variable = { which = miaphysite_unctionist_blamed value = -1 }
			}
			if = {
				limit = { check_variable = { which = miaphysite_sonsofgrace_blamed value = 3 } }
				change_variable = { which = miaphysite_sonsofgrace_blamed value = -1 }
			}
			if = {
				limit = { check_variable = { which = miaphysite_zakristos_blamed value = 3 } }
				change_variable = { which = miaphysite_zakristos_blamed value = -1 }
			}
			if = {
				limit = { check_variable = { which = miaphysite_stephanite_blamed value = 3 } }
				change_variable = { which = miaphysite_stephanite_blamed value = -1 }
			}
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = dg_miaphysite.128.unity #Ban Unity
		ai_chance = { factor = 18 }
		trigger = { check_variable = { which = miaphysite_unity_blamed value = 3 } }
		hidden_effect = { set_variable = { which = miaphysite_unity_blamed value = 0 } }
		set_country_flag = miaphysite_unity_banned
		set_country_flag = miaphysite_unity_exiled
		every_owned_province = {
			limit = { has_province_modifier = monastery_unity }
			remove_province_modifier = monastery_unity
			hidden_effect = {
				set_variable = { which = added_unrest value = 2 }
				add_base_unrest = yes
			}
			custom_tooltip = added_unrest_2
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = dg_miaphysite.128.unctionist #Ban Unctionist
		ai_chance = { factor = 18 }
		trigger = { check_variable = { which = miaphysite_unctionist_blamed value = 3 } }
		add_adm_power = -10
		hidden_effect = { set_variable = { which = miaphysite_unctionist_blamed value = 0 } }
		set_country_flag = miaphysite_unctionist_banned
		set_country_flag = miaphysite_unctionist_exiled
		every_owned_province = {
			limit = { has_province_modifier = monastery_unctionist }
			remove_province_modifier = monastery_unctionist
			hidden_effect = {
				set_variable = { which = added_unrest value = 2 }
				add_base_unrest = yes
			}
			custom_tooltip = added_unrest_2
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = dg_miaphysite.128.zakristos #Ban Zakristos
		ai_chance = { factor = 18 }
		trigger = { check_variable = { which = miaphysite_zakristos_blamed value = 3 } }
		add_adm_power = -10
		hidden_effect = { set_variable = { which = miaphysite_zakristos_blamed value = 0 } }
		set_country_flag = miaphysite_zakristos_banned
		set_country_flag = miaphysite_zakristos_exiled
		every_owned_province = {
			limit = { has_province_modifier = monastery_zakristos }
			remove_province_modifier = monastery_zakristos
			hidden_effect = {
				set_variable = { which = added_unrest value = 2 }
				add_base_unrest = yes
			}
			custom_tooltip = added_unrest_2
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = dg_miaphysite.128.stephanite #Ban Stephanites
		ai_chance = { factor = 18 }
		trigger = { check_variable = { which = miaphysite_stephanite_blamed value = 3 } }
		add_adm_power = -10
		hidden_effect = { set_variable = { which = miaphysite_stephanite_blamed value = 0 } }
		set_country_flag = miaphysite_stephanite_banned
		set_country_flag = miaphysite_stephanite_exiled

			remove_province_modifier = monastery_stephanite
			hidden_effect = {
				set_variable = { which = added_unrest value = 2 }
				add_base_unrest = yes
			}
			custom_tooltip = added_unrest_2
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = dg_miaphysite.128.sonsofgrace #Ban the Children of Grace
		ai_chance = { factor = 18 }
		trigger = { check_variable = { which = miaphysite_sonsofgrace_blamed value = 3 } }
		add_adm_power = -10
		hidden_effect = { set_variable = { which = miaphysite_sonsofgrace_blamed value = 0 } }
		set_country_flag = miaphysite_sonsofgrace_banned
		set_country_flag = miaphysite_sonsofgrace_exiled
		every_owned_province = {
			limit = { has_province_modifier = monastery_sonsofgrace }
			remove_province_modifier = monastery_sonsofgrace
			hidden_effect = {
				set_variable = { which = added_unrest value = 2 }
				add_base_unrest = yes
			}
			custom_tooltip = added_unrest_2
		}
	}
}

	id = dg_miaphysite.129
	title = dg_miaphysite.129.t
	desc = dg_miaphysite.129.d

		}

			clr_country_flag = miaphysite_zakristos_banned
		}

			clr_country_flag = miaphysite_sonsofgrace_banned
		}

		}
		clr_country_flag = miaphysite_unity_exiled
		clr_country_flag = miaphysite_stephanite_exiled
		clr_country_flag = miaphysite_unctionist_exiled
		clr_country_flag = miaphysite_zakristos_exiled

		}

		}
	}
}

#134 Ichege/Archpriest
#xxx
#During the ongoing dispute over Christology that had split the Ethiopian Church into a number of hostile factions, Shewa had embraced the doctrine of the Sost Lidet in opposition to the theory of Wold Qib, which was embraced in the north. The Sost Lidet was also embraced by the influential monastery of Debre Libanos, located in Shewa. When Sahle Selassie sought to strengthen his power over the Shewan church by appointing men loyal to himself as trusties of the local monasteries?n act that brought the opposition not only of the monks themselves, but also of the Ichege, the abbot of the monastery of Debre Libanos and the second most powerful churchman in Ethiopia. Facing the threat of excommunication, Sahle Selassie relented and on 24 November 1841 dismissed his appointees?nly to find himself under attack by Shewan supporters of the Wold Qib in Menz, Marra Biete, and other districts. At the moment the monarch managed to quiet this controversy, the arrival of a new Abuna, Salama III reawoke the resistance of the followers of the Wold Qib, and the new Abuna excommunicated Sahle Selassie in 1845. Despite the intervention of Imperial Regent, Ras Ali II, Abuna Salama refused to lift the interdict, and Ras Ali finally arrested the Abuna in 1846 and banished him from Gondar.

#The liqa kahnat/ichege (archpriest) accompanied the embassy of Dom Rodrigo de Lima on its return to Portugal in 1527 to establish an alliance.  There he was interrogated about the Ethiopian rite.  Circumcision, dietary prohibitions, keeping of the Sabbath, priestly marriage and yearly rebaptism were all seen as Jewish.

country_event = { #137 - The Stephanite Legacy (converts hidden Protestants to Protestants upon meeting them)
	
	id = dg_miaphysite.137
	title = dg_miaphysite.137.t
	desc = dg_miaphysite.137.d
	picture = miaphysite_catholic_missionary_saffron
	
	trigger = {
		has_country_flag = stephanite_foundation
		has_country_flag = met_other_christians
		NOT = { has_country_flag = stephanite_legacy }
		OR = {
			any_neighbor_country = { religion = protestant }
			any_ally = { religion = protestant }
			check_variable = { which = population_protestant value = 0.5 }
		}
		religion = coptic
		is_religion_enabled = protestant
	}
	
	mean_time_to_happen = { months = 1 }
	
	option = {
		name = dg_miaphysite.137.a
		set_country_flag = stephanite_legacy
		hidden_effect = {
			every_owned_province = {
				change_variable = { which = protestant which = stephanites }
				subtract_variable = { which = province_religion which = stephanites }
			}
		}
	}
}

country_event = { #141 - The Synodos (14th century Ethiopia)
	
	id = dg_miaphysite.141
	title = dg_miaphysite.141.t
	desc = dg_miaphysite.141.d
	picture = miaphysite_writing_saffron
	
	trigger = {
		religion = coptic
		NOT = { has_country_flag = miaphysite_synodos }
		is_at_war = no
		OR = {
			any_neighbor_country = { any_owned_province = { region = egypt_region } }
			any_owned_province = { region = egypt_region }
		}
		is_year = 1250 #Probably written in early 1200s
		OR = {
			advisor = theologian
			has_country_flag = patriarch_theologian
			has_country_flag = patriarch_controversial
			egyptian_culture_trigger = yes
		}
	}

		months = 50

			factor = 0.5
		}

		}
		else = {

		}

		dg_add_prestige_small = yes
		if = {
			limit = { piety = 0.60 }
			add_adm_power = 25
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = { piety = 0.20 }
			add_adm_power = 20
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = { piety = -0.20 }
			add_adm_power = 15
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = { piety = -0.60 }
			add_adm_power = 10
		}
		else = {
			add_adm_power = 5
		}
	}

country_event = { #143 - Uprooting Paganism at Court (1434-68 Ethiopia)
	
	id = dg_miaphysite.143
	title = dg_miaphysite.143.t
	desc = dg_miaphysite.143.d
	picture = miaphysite_witchdoctor_saffron
	
	trigger = {
		religion_group = christian
		capital_scope = { check_variable = { which = animism value = 2 } }
		NOT = { months_of_ruling = 60 }
		has_heir = yes
		is_at_war = no
		NOT = { has_country_modifier = miaphysite_strict_christian_rules }
		OR = { has_regency = no has_consort_regency = yes }
		government = monarchy
		NOT = { has_country_flag = uprooted_paganism_at_court }
		capital_scope = { NOT = { has_province_modifier = religious_scandal_province } }
	}
	
	mean_time_to_happen = {
		
		years = 12
		
		modifier = {
			advisor = inquisitor
			factor = 0.5
		}
		modifier = {
			has_country_flag = patriarch_zealous
			factor = 0.5
		}
	}
	
	immediate = { set_country_flag = uprooted_paganism_at_court }
	
	option = {
		name = dg_miaphysite.143.a #Root it out even at the highest levels
		ai_chance = { factor = 60 }
		add_adm_power = -10
		kill_advisor = random
		set_country_flag = pagan_assassination_target
		if = {
			limit = {
				NOT = { has_country_modifier = religious_tolerance }
				NOT = { has_country_modifier = religious_intolerance }
			}
			add_piety = 0.20
		}
		if = {
			limit = { has_country_modifier = religious_tolerance }
			remove_country_modifier = religious_tolerance
			add_piety = 0.40
		}
		add_country_modifier = { name = religious_intolerance duration = 1000 }
		capital_scope = {
			custom_tooltip = coptic_10
			add_province_modifier = { name = religious_scandal_province duration = 3000 }
			hidden_effect = {
				change_variable = { which = animism value = -2 }
				change_variable = { which = converts value = 2 }
			}
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = dg_miaphysite.143.b #Get rid of the most blatant offenders
		ai_chance = { factor = 30 }
		remove_advisor = random
		capital_scope = {
			add_province_modifier = { name = religious_scandal_province duration = 500 }
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = dg_miaphysite.143.c #Live and let live
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 10
			modifier = {
				patriarch_authority = 0.80
				factor = 0
			}
			modifier = {
				patriarch_authority = 0.60
				factor = 0.5
			}
			modifier = {
				NOT = { patriarch_authority = 0.40 }
				factor = 2
			}
			modifier = {
				NOT = { patriarch_authority = 0.20 }
				factor = 2
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = { patriarch_authority = 0.80 }
			add_country_modifier = { name = unhappy_church_powerful duration = 1000 }
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = { patriarch_authority = 0.60 }
			add_country_modifier = { name = unhappy_church_strong duration = 1000 }
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = { patriarch_authority = 0.40 }
			add_country_modifier = { name = unhappy_church_moderate duration = 1000 }
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = { patriarch_authority = 0.20 }
			add_country_modifier = { name = unhappy_church_weak duration = 1000 }
		}
		else = {
			add_country_modifier = { name = unhappy_church_impotent duration = 1000 }
		}
		if = {
			limit = { NOT = { has_country_modifier = religious_intolerance } NOT = { has_country_modifier = religious_tolerance } }
			add_country_modifier = { name = religious_tolerance duration = 1000 }
			add_piety = -0.20
		}
		if = {
			limit = { has_country_modifier = religious_intolerance }
			remove_country_modifier = religious_intolerance
			add_piety = -0.20
		}
	}
}

country_event = { #151 - The Cult of Zakristos
	
	id = dg_miaphysite.151
	title = dg_miaphysite.151.t
	desc = dg_miaphysite.151.d
	picture = miaphysite_prophet_disciples_saffron
	
	trigger = {
		religion = coptic
		is_year = 1500
		NOT = { has_global_flag = miaphysite_cult_of_zakristos }
		OR = {
			has_country_modifier = religious_controversy
			has_country_flag = patriarch_controversial
			has_country_flag = patriarch_corrupt
			NOT = { stability = 0 }
		}
		num_of_cities = 2
	}
	
	mean_time_to_happen = {
		
		years = 83
		
		modifier = {
			ai = no
			factor = 0.5
		}
		modifier = {
			NOT = { num_of_cities = 3 }
			factor = 1.4
		}
		modifier = {
			NOT = { num_of_cities = 5 }
			factor = 1.4
		}
		modifier = {
			NOT = { num_of_cities = 9 }
			factor = 1.4
		}
		modifier = {
			has_country_modifier = religious_intolerance
			factor = 1.4
		}
		modifier = {
			has_country_modifier = religious_tolerance
			factor = 0.7
		}
	}
	
	immediate = { set_global_flag = miaphysite_cult_of_zakristos }
	
	option = {
		name = dg_miaphysite.151.a #Leave them alone
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 70
			modifier = {
				has_country_modifier = religious_tolerance
				factor = 1.4
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				NOT = { has_country_modifier = religious_tolerance }
				NOT = { has_country_modifier = religious_intolerance }
			}
			add_piety = -0.20
		}
		if = {
			limit = { has_country_modifier = religious_intolerance }
			remove_country_modifier = religious_intolerance
			add_piety = -0.40
		}
		add_country_modifier = { name = religious_tolerance duration = 1000 }
		random_owned_province = {
			limit = { has_owner_religion = yes is_capital = no }
			set_province_flag = cult_of_zakristos
			add_province_modifier = { name = religious_scandal_province duration = 2000 }
			hidden_effect = {
				change_variable = { which = heretics value = 2 }
				change_variable = { which = province_religion value = -2 }
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					has_country_flag = patriarch_controversial
					has_country_flag = patriarch_hostile
				}
			}
			random = {
				chance = 50
				if = {
					limit = { patriarch_authority = 0.80 }
					add_country_modifier = { name = unhappy_church_powerful duration = 1000 }
				}
				else_if = {
					limit = { patriarch_authority = 0.60 }
					add_country_modifier = { name = unhappy_church_strong duration = 1000 }
				}
				else_if = {
					limit = { patriarch_authority = 0.40 }
					add_country_modifier = { name = unhappy_church_moderate duration = 1000 }
				}
				else_if = {
					limit = { patriarch_authority = 0.20 }
					add_country_modifier = { name = unhappy_church_weak duration = 1000 }
				}
				else = {
					add_country_modifier = { name = unhappy_church_impotent duration = 1000 }
				}
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = { has_country_flag = patriarch_zealous }
			if = {
				limit = { patriarch_authority = 0.80 }
				add_country_modifier = { name = unhappy_church_powerful duration = 1000 }
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = { patriarch_authority = 0.60 }
				add_country_modifier = { name = unhappy_church_strong duration = 1000 }
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = { patriarch_authority = 0.40 }
				add_country_modifier = { name = unhappy_church_moderate duration = 1000 }
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = { patriarch_authority = 0.20 }
				add_country_modifier = { name = unhappy_church_weak duration = 1000 }
			}
			else = {
				add_country_modifier = { name = unhappy_church_impotent duration = 1000 }
			}
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = dg_miaphysite.151.b #Slaughter the heretics
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 30
			modifier = {
				has_country_modifier = religious_intolerance
				factor = 1.4
			}
		}
		add_mil_power = -25
		if = {
			limit = {
				NOT = { has_country_modifier = religious_tolerance }
				NOT = { has_country_modifier = religious_intolerance }
			}
			add_piety = 0.20
		}
		if = {
			limit = { has_country_modifier = religious_tolerance }
			remove_country_modifier = religious_tolerance
			add_piety = 0.40
		}
		add_country_modifier = { name = religious_intolerance duration = 1000 }
		random_owned_province = {
			limit = { has_owner_religion = yes is_capital = no } #Should pick a fortified place...?  Or add a temporary fort?
			set_province_flag = zakristos_death
			hidden_effect = {
				set_variable = { which = added_unrest value = 5 }
				add_base_unrest = yes
			}
			custom_tooltip = added_unrest_5
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					has_country_flag = patriarch_controversial
					has_country_flag = patriarch_hostile
				}
			}
			random = {
				chance = 50
				if = {
					limit = { patriarch_authority = 0.80 }
					add_country_modifier = { name = unhappy_church_powerful duration = 1000 }
				}
				else_if = {
					limit = { patriarch_authority = 0.60 }
					add_country_modifier = { name = unhappy_church_strong duration = 1000 }
				}
				else_if = {
					limit = { patriarch_authority = 0.40 }
					add_country_modifier = { name = unhappy_church_moderate duration = 1000 }
				}
				else_if = {
					limit = { patriarch_authority = 0.20 }
					add_country_modifier = { name = unhappy_church_weak duration = 1000 }
				}
				else = {
					add_country_modifier = { name = unhappy_church_impotent duration = 1000 }
				}
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = { has_country_flag = patriarch_theologian }
			if = {
				limit = { patriarch_authority = 0.80 }
				add_country_modifier = { name = unhappy_church_powerful duration = 1000 }
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = { patriarch_authority = 0.60 }
				add_country_modifier = { name = unhappy_church_strong duration = 1000 }
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = { patriarch_authority = 0.40 }
				add_country_modifier = { name = unhappy_church_moderate duration = 1000 }
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = { patriarch_authority = 0.20 }
				add_country_modifier = { name = unhappy_church_weak duration = 1000 }
			}
			else = {
				add_country_modifier = { name = unhappy_church_impotent duration = 1000 }
			}
		}
	}
}

		}
		modifier = {

			factor = 0.5
		}
		modifier = {
			owner = { war_exhaustion = 8 }
			factor = 0.5
		}
		modifier = {
			owner = { NOT = { manpower_percentage = 0.50 } }
			factor = 0.7
		}
		modifier = {
			owner = { NOT = { manpower_percentage = 0.25 } }
			factor = 0.7
		}
	}
	
	immediate = { clr_province_flag = cult_of_zakristos }
	
	option = {
		name = dg_miaphysite.152.a
		hidden_effect = {
			set_variable = { which = added_unrest value = 10 }
			add_base_unrest = yes
		}
		custom_tooltip = added_unrest_10
		spawn_rebels = { type = heretic_rebels size = 1 }
		change_controller = REB
		set_province_flag = zakristos_stronghold
	}
}

province_event = { #153 - Zakristos in Chains
	
	id = dg_miaphysite.153
	title = dg_miaphysite.153.t
	desc = dg_miaphysite.153.d
	picture = miaphysite_heretics_burning_saffron
	
	trigger = {
		has_province_flag = zakristos_stronghold
		controlled_by = owner
	}
	
	mean_time_to_happen = { months = 1 }
	
	immediate = { clr_province_flag = zakristos_stronghold }
	
	option = {
		name = dg_miaphysite.153.a #Execute him
		hidden_effect = {
			set_variable = { which = added_unrest value = -10 }
			add_base_unrest = yes
		}
		custom_tooltip = added_unrest_10
		set_province_flag = zakristos_death
	}
	option = {
		name = dg_miaphysite.153.b #Execute him and all of his followers
		hidden_effect = {
			set_variable = { which = added_unrest value = 10 }
			add_base_unrest = yes
		}
		custom_tooltip = added_unrest_10
		owner = {
			subtract_stability_1 = yes
			if = {
				limit = {
					NOT = { has_country_modifier = religious_tolerance }
					NOT = { has_country_modifier = religious_intolerance }
				}
				add_piety = 0.20
			}
			if = {
				limit = { has_country_modifier = religious_tolerance }
				remove_country_modifier = religious_tolerance
				add_piety = 0.40
			}
			add_country_modifier = { name = religious_intolerance duration = 1000 }
		}
	}
}

province_event = { #154 - Zakristos Reborn
	
	id = dg_miaphysite.154
	title = dg_miaphysite.154.t
	desc = dg_miaphysite.154.d
	picture = miaphysite_prophet_disciples_saffron
	
	trigger = {
		has_province_flag = zakristos_death
		had_province_flag = { flag = zakristos_death days = 3000 }
	}
	
	mean_time_to_happen = { months = 50 }
	
	immediate = { clr_province_flag = zakristos_death }
	
	option = {
		name = dg_miaphysite.154.c #Persecute the cult
		ai_chance = { factor = 60 }
		hidden_effect = {
			set_variable = { which = added_unrest value = 10 }
			add_base_unrest = yes
		}
		custom_tooltip = added_unrest_10
	}
	option = {
		name = dg_miaphysite.154.a #Leave them alone
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 10
			modifier = {
				owner = { NOT = { religion_group = christian } }
				factor = 5
			}
			modifier = {
				owner = { has_country_flag = patriarch_zealous }
				factor = 0.5
			}
		}
		add_province_modifier = { name = monastery_zakristos duration = 10000 }
		add_province_modifier = { name = religious_scandal_province duration = 2000 }
		owner = {
			set_country_flag = zakristos_foundation
			if = {
				limit = {
					NOT = { has_country_modifier = religious_tolerance }
					NOT = { has_country_modifier = religious_intolerance }
				}
				add_piety = -0.20
			}
			if = {
				limit = { has_country_modifier = religious_intolerance }
				remove_country_modifier = religious_intolerance
				add_piety = -0.40
			}
			add_country_modifier = { name = religious_tolerance duration = 1000 }
			random_owned_province = {
				limit = {
					has_province_modifier = monastery_zakristos
					NOT = { has_province_flag = unity_center }
					NOT = { has_province_flag = unctionist_center }
					NOT = { has_province_flag = stephanite_center }
					NOT = { has_province_flag = sonsofgrace_center }
				}
				set_province_flag = zakristos_center
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					has_country_flag = patriarch_theologian
					has_country_flag = patriarch_hostile
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = { patriarch_authority = 0.80 }
				add_country_modifier = { name = unhappy_church_powerful duration = 1000 }
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = { patriarch_authority = 0.60 }
				add_country_modifier = { name = unhappy_church_strong duration = 1000 }
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = { patriarch_authority = 0.40 }
				add_country_modifier = { name = unhappy_church_moderate duration = 1000 }
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = { patriarch_authority = 0.20 }
				add_country_modifier = { name = unhappy_church_weak duration = 1000 }
			}
			else = {
				add_country_modifier = { name = unhappy_church_impotent duration = 1000 }
			}
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = dg_miaphysite.154.b #Round them up and execute them
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 30
			modifier = {
				has_country_flag = patriarch_theologian
				factor = 0.5
			}
		}
		owner = {
			add_mil_power = -25
			if = {
				limit = {
					NOT = { has_country_modifier = religious_tolerance }
					NOT = { has_country_modifier = religious_intolerance }
				}
				add_piety = 0.20
			}
			if = {
				limit = { has_country_modifier = religious_tolerance }
				remove_country_modifier = religious_tolerance
				add_piety = 0.40
			}
			add_country_modifier = { name = religious_intolerance duration = 1000 }
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					has_country_flag = patriarch_theologian
					has_country_flag = patriarch_hostile
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = { patriarch_authority = 0.80 }
				add_country_modifier = { name = unhappy_church_powerful duration = 1000 }
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = { patriarch_authority = 0.60 }
				add_country_modifier = { name = unhappy_church_strong duration = 1000 }
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = { patriarch_authority = 0.40 }
				add_country_modifier = { name = unhappy_church_moderate duration = 1000 }
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = { patriarch_authority = 0.20 }
				add_country_modifier = { name = unhappy_church_weak duration = 1000 }
			}
			else = {
				add_country_modifier = { name = unhappy_church_impotent duration = 1000 }
			}
		}
	}
}

country_event = { #161 - A Meeting with Heretics (16th century)
	
	id = dg_miaphysite.161
	title = dg_miaphysite.161.t
	desc = dg_miaphysite.161.d
	picture = miaphysite_catholic_missionary_saffron
	
	trigger = {
		religion = coptic
		NOT = { has_country_flag = met_other_christians }
		any_known_country = {
			OR = {
				is_neighbor_of = ROOT
				alliance_with = ROOT
				marriage_with = ROOT
			}
			any_owned_province = { africa_continent_trigger = no asia_continent_trigger = no }
			religion_group = christian
			NOT = { religion = ROOT }
		}
	}
	
	mean_time_to_happen = { months = 6 }
	
	immediate = { set_country_flag = met_other_christians }
	
	option = {
		name = dg_miaphysite.161.a
	}
}

					change_variable = { which = sympathy_to_old_religion value = 20 }
				}
				capital_scope = {
					custom_tooltip = chaldean_10
					hidden_effect = { change_variable = { which = chaldean value = 2 } change_variable = { which = province_religion value = -2 } }
				}
			}
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = dg_miaphysite.163.c #Send them home
		trigger = { FROM = { has_country_flag = prester_john_missionaries@ROOT } }
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 30
			modifier = {
				has_country_flag = miaphysite_monastic_demonstration
				factor = 1.4
			}
			modifier = {
				has_country_flag = miaphysite_monastic_assassination
				factor = 1.4
			}
		}
		add_prestige = -1
		clr_country_flag = miaphysite_expedition_missionaries
		random_country = {
			limit = { has_country_flag = prester_john_missionaries@ROOT }
			random_list = {
				80 = {
					set_country_flag = prester_john_expulsion
					country_event = { id = dg_miaphysite.166 days = 180 }
				}
				20 = { country_event = { id = dg_miaphysite.164 days = 180 } }
			}
		}
	}

			limit = { has_country_flag = prester_john_expulsion }
			custom_tooltip = dg_miaphysite.166.expelled

		}

			limit = {
				NOT = { has_country_flag = prester_john_expulsion }
				has_country_flag = prester_john_mistreatment
			}
			custom_tooltip = dg_miaphysite.166.imprisoned
			set_country_flag = prester_john_expedition_imprisoned
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				NOT = { has_country_flag = prester_john_expulsion }
				NOT = { has_country_flag = prester_john_mistreatment }
				has_country_flag = prester_john_gifts
			}
			custom_tooltip = dg_miaphysite.166.rewarded
			set_country_flag = prester_john_expedition_rewarded
		}
	}
	
	option = {
		name = dg_miaphysite.166.a #Welcome home
		if = {
			limit = { has_country_flag = prester_john_expulsion }
			clr_country_flag = prester_john_expulsion
			add_opinion = { who = FROM modifier = expelled_expedition }
		}
		if = {
			limit = { has_country_flag = prester_john_mistreatment }
			clr_country_flag = prester_john_mistreatment
			add_opinion = { who = FROM modifier = imprisoned_expedition }
		}
		if = {
			limit = { has_country_flag = prester_john_gifts }
			clr_country_flag = prester_john_gifts
			add_treasury = 50
			add_opinion = { who = FROM modifier = rewarded_expedition }
		}
	}
}

country_event = { #168 - Monastic Demonstration (1716-21)
	
	id = dg_miaphysite.168
	title = dg_miaphysite.168.t
	desc = dg_miaphysite.168.d
	picture = miaphysite_heretics_saffron
	
	trigger = {
		religion = coptic
		has_country_modifier = prester_john_missionaries
		NOT = { check_variable = { which = monastic_decline value = 5 } }
	}
	
	mean_time_to_happen = {
		
		years = 8
		
		modifier = {
			check_variable = { which = monastic_decline value = 1 }
			factor = 1.4
		}
		modifier = {
			check_variable = { which = monastic_decline value = 2 }
			factor = 1.4
		}
		modifier = {
			check_variable = { which = monastic_decline value = 3 }
			factor = 1.4
		}
		modifier = {
			check_variable = { which = monastic_decline value = 4 }
			factor = 1.4
		}
		modifier = {
			piety = 0.60
			factor = 0.7
		}
		modifier = {
			piety = 0.20
			factor = 0.7
		}
		modifier = {
			NOT = { piety = -0.20 }
			factor = 1.4
		}
		modifier = {
			NOT = { piety = -0.60 }
			factor = 1.4
		}
	}
	
	option = {
		name = dg_miaphysite.168.e #Try to accommodate both sides
		ai_chance = { factor = 40 }
		if = {
			limit = { NOT = { has_country_modifier = religious_intolerance } NOT = { has_country_modifier = religious_tolerance } }
			add_country_modifier = { name = religious_tolerance duration = 1000 }
			add_piety = -0.20
		}
		if = {
			limit = { has_country_modifier = religious_intolerance }
			remove_country_modifier = religious_intolerance
			add_piety = -0.20
		}
		add_adm_power = -10
		hidden_effect = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					OR = { has_regency = no has_consort_regency = yes }
					OR = {
						has_country_flag = patriarch_hostile
						has_country_flag = patriarch_corrupt
						has_country_flag = patriarch_controversial
					}
					NOT = { has_country_flag = miaphysite_monastic_assassination }
				}
				random = {
					chance = 10
					country_event = { id = dg_miaphysite.169 days = 60 }
				}
			}
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = dg_miaphysite.168.c #Send the foreigners into exile
		ai_chance = { factor = 20 }
		if = {
			limit = {
				NOT = { has_country_modifier = religious_tolerance }
				NOT = { has_country_modifier = religious_intolerance }
			}
			add_piety = 0.20
		}
		if = {
			limit = { has_country_modifier = religious_tolerance }
			remove_country_modifier = religious_tolerance
			add_piety = 0.40
		}
		add_country_modifier = { name = religious_intolerance duration = 1000 }
		remove_country_modifier = prester_john_missionaries
		add_prestige = -5
		clr_country_flag = miaphysite_expedition_missionaries
		hidden_effect = { multiply_variable = { which = sympathy_to_old_religion value = 0.5 } }
		random_country = {
			limit = { has_country_flag = prester_john_missionaries@ROOT }
			random_list = {
				80 = {
					set_country_flag = prester_john_expulsion
					country_event = { id = dg_miaphysite.166 days = 180 }
				}
				20 = { country_event = { id = dg_miaphysite.164 days = 180 } }
			}
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = dg_miaphysite.168.a #Slaughter the monks
		ai_chance = { factor = 20 }
		if = {
			limit = { piety = 0.20 }
			add_country_modifier = { name = religious_scandal_country_strong duration = 1000 }
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = { piety = -0.20 }
			add_country_modifier = { name = religious_scandal_country duration = 1000 }
		}
		else = {
			add_country_modifier = { name = religious_scandal_country_weak duration = 1000 }
		}
		if = {
			limit = { NOT = { has_country_flag = patriarch_hostile } }
			random = {
				chance = 50
				custom_tooltip = patriarch_becomes_hostile
				set_country_flag = patriarch_hostile
				clr_country_flag = patriarch_controversial
				clr_country_flag = patriarch_zealous
				clr_country_flag = patriarch_obedient
				clr_country_flag = patriarch_theologian
				clr_country_flag = patriarch_corrupt
			}
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					OR = { has_regency = no has_consort_regency = yes }
					NOT = { has_country_flag = miaphysite_monastic_assassination }
				}
				random = {
					chance = 20
					country_event = { id = dg_miaphysite.169 days = 60 }
				}
			}
		}
	}
	#option = {
	#	name = dg_miaphysite.168.b #Send the monks into exile
	#	ai_chance = { factor = 20 }
	#	add_adm_power = -10
	#	}
}

			limit = {
				any_owned_province = { has_province_modifier = monastery_stephanite }
				NOT = { has_country_flag = miaphysite_doctrine_stephanite }
			}
			clr_country_flag = miaphysite_doctrine_sonsofgrace
			clr_country_flag = miaphysite_doctrine_unctionist
			clr_country_flag = miaphysite_doctrine_zakristos
			set_country_flag = miaphysite_doctrine_stephanite
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				any_owned_province = { has_province_modifier = monastery_zakristos }
				NOT = { has_country_flag = miaphysite_doctrine_zakristos }
			}
			clr_country_flag = miaphysite_doctrine_sonsofgrace
			clr_country_flag = miaphysite_doctrine_unctionist
			set_country_flag = miaphysite_doctrine_zakristos
			clr_country_flag = miaphysite_doctrine_stephanite
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				any_owned_province = { has_province_modifier = monastery_sonsofgrace }
				NOT = { has_country_flag = miaphysite_doctrine_sonsofgrace }
			}
			set_country_flag = miaphysite_doctrine_sonsofgrace
			clr_country_flag = miaphysite_doctrine_unctionist
			clr_country_flag = miaphysite_doctrine_zakristos
			clr_country_flag = miaphysite_doctrine_stephanite
		}
		#Really ought to change which faction is being supported
		add_stability_1 = yes
		if = {
			limit = { NOT = { check_variable = { which = church_property value = 10 } } }
			hidden_effect = { change_variable = { which = church_property value = 1 } }
			add_patriarch_authority = 0.05
		}
		if = {
			limit = { check_variable = { which = monastic_decline value = 1 } }
			change_variable = { which = monastic_decline value = -1 }
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_country_flag = patriarch_hostile
				has_country_flag = patriarch_controversial
			}
			clr_country_flag = patriarch_hostile
			clr_country_flag = patriarch_controversial
			set_country_flag = patriarch_obedient
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = dg_miaphysite.169.b #Restrict the monks
		ai_chance = { factor = 40 }
		add_adm_power = -10
		custom_tooltip = patriarch_becomes_hostile
		set_country_flag = patriarch_hostile
		clr_country_flag = patriarch_controversial
		clr_country_flag = patriarch_zealous
		clr_country_flag = patriarch_obedient
		clr_country_flag = patriarch_theologian
		clr_country_flag = patriarch_corrupt
		hidden_effect = {
			change_variable = { which = monastic_decline value = 1 }
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = dg_miaphysite.169.c #Look elsewhere for answers
		ai_chance = { factor = 20 }
		add_prestige = -5
	}
	after = {
		dg_patriarch_triggers = yes
	}
}

#170 - The Illness of the [Negus] (17xx - asked for a foreign medic, who turned out to be a Jesuit; after missionaries were banned)
#xxx

#171 - A trained Medic
#xxx



province_event = { #177 - Flight of the Patriarch - Antioch
	
	id = dg_miaphysite.177
	title = dg_miaphysite.177.t
	desc = dg_miaphysite.177.d
	picture = orthodox_patriarch_migration
	
	hidden = yes
	
	trigger = {
		has_province_flag = miaphysite_catholicos_of_antioch
		has_province_modifier = coptic_patriarchate_vacant
		antioch_patriarch_area = {
			owner = { religion = coptic NOT = { tag = ROOT } }
			NOT = { has_province_flag = coptic_patriarchate }
		}
	}
	
	mean_time_to_happen = { months = 50 }
	
	immediate = {
		hidden_effect = {
			every_neighbor_province = {
				every_neighbor_province = {
					every_neighbor_province = {
						limit = {
							province_group = antioch_patriarch_area
							owner = { religion = coptic }
							NOT = { has_province_flag = coptic_patriarchate }
						}
						set_variable = { which = patriarch_flight value = 1 }
					}
				}
			}
			every_neighbor_province = {
				every_neighbor_province = {
					limit = {
						province_group = antioch_patriarch_area
						owner = { religion = coptic }
						NOT = { has_province_flag = coptic_patriarchate }
					}
					set_variable = { which = patriarch_flight value = 2 }
				}
			}
			every_neighbor_province = {
				limit = {
					province_group = antioch_patriarch_area
					owner = { religion = coptic }
					NOT = { has_province_flag = coptic_patriarchate }
				}
				set_variable = { which = patriarch_flight value = 3 }
			}
			antioch_patriarch_area = {
				limit = {
					owner = { religion = coptic }
					NOT = { has_province_flag = coptic_patriarchate }
				}
				change_variable = { which = patriarch_flight value = 1 }
				if = {
					limit = { culture_group = ROOT }
					change_variable = { which = patriarch_flight value = 2 }
				}
				if = {
					limit = { culture = ROOT }
					change_variable = { which = patriarch_flight value = 2 }
				}
				if = {
					limit = { religion = coptic }
					change_variable = { which = patriarch_flight value = 1 }
				}
				if = {
					limit = { has_province_flag = miaphysite_catholicos_of_jerusalem }
					set_variable = { which = patriarch_flight value = 0 }
				}
				if = {
					limit = { owner = { any_owned_province = { province_id = ROOT } } }
					set_variable = { which = patriarch_flight value = 0 }
				}
				if = {
					limit = { owner = { ai = no has_country_flag = returned_patriarch_to_bondage } }
					set_variable = { which = patriarch_flight value = 0 }
				}
			}
		}
	}
	
	option = {
		name = dg_miaphysite.167.a
		random_province = {
			limit = {
				all_province = {
					province_group = antioch_patriarch_area
					OR = {
						NOT = { check_variable = { which = patriarch_flight which = PREV } }
						is_variable_equal = { which = patriarch_flight which = PREV }
					}
				}
			}
			province_event = { id = dg_miaphysite.043 days = 30 }
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			regiongroup = {
				region = {
					set_variable = { which = patriarch_flight value = 0 }
				}
			}
		}
	}
}
